Commentary

Respectful Observation of the Urgent Sino-Soviet Situation 14

At a time when negotiations on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway are intermittent, Sino-Soviet relations have once again shown a dangerous state. According to Havas News Agency, Japanese military police have arrested more than 20 Russian employees at the Suifenhe Railway Station and other stations, and are preparing to expand the scope of the arrest. It is believed that this is a planned action, not a mere coincidence. Moreover, Soviet aircraft have been constantly conducting reconnaissance on the Soviet-Manchurian border, which has also aroused protests from both the Japanese and puppet sides. As for the Japanese side's claim that the Soviet side is moving border markers, although it comes from Japanese propaganda, it cannot be fully believed. However, after this publicity, how much seriousness will be added is to be expected. The Sino-Soviet sides have been displaying their military strength and preparing for the worst. The urgency of the situation has not started today. At the end of last year, someone inspected both ends of the Chinese Eastern Railway and witnessed the heated preparation of the Sino-Soviet war, saying that a war could not be avoided this summer, as if a major war already had a motive.

Since the beginning of this year, the possibility of war has become more and more obvious. First, Japan is actively building railways and highways in the northeastern provinces. In addition to the completion of the Duntugou section of the Ji-He Railway, there is also a plan for the so-called seven major railway trunk lines. Among them, the Rehe Railway and the Tao-Suo Railway are the most militarily significant. The former is used to control Inner Mongolia, and the latter is used to guard the Xing'an Mountains. The rest, such as the highways that run horizontally and vertically across the entire territory, are also aimed at war in determining their construction routes. Second, the Japanese army recently convened a meeting in Chengde. Most of the participants belonged to the backbone cadres, and the person in charge was the famous aggressor Doihara. It is obvious that the Japanese are increasing their troops along the Great Wall. Grabbing Inner Mongolia is particularly determined. Considering their intention, it is nothing more than to take two approaches. On the one hand, they want to lure the Mongols into their arms. On the other hand, they take the opportunity to send troops straight to Outer Mongolia, as a prelude to the war against the Soviet Union. Third, Japan had heavy troops along the Chinese Eastern Railway. This spring, they used the name of troop rotation to move the 3rd and 16th Divisions to Harbin, Heilongjiang and other places, and attached special units, such as air squadrons and tank squadrons. Everything was available to form a wartime organization. The number of troops stationed and the details of the distribution are all strictly confidential and never leaked. From the tension of its actions, it can be seen that it is actively preparing for war. Fourth, although Japan intends to go to war, it is still afraid of air raids. Vladivostok and Japan's Keihin giant town are very close, making defense even more difficult. Therefore, it is stepping up air defense efforts. If it is not clear that war is inevitable, why bother to do this urgently.

Because of these various reasons, one feels that the Sino-Soviet situation is becoming more and more urgent. However, since the Soviet Union implemented the second five-year plan, it has focused on domestic construction, so it has tried its best to seek stability in all directions. This is the case with Western Europe, and the same is true with the Far East. Although it sometimes shows its edge, targeting Japan, it is only a kind of demonstration and warning, and it is by no means intentional to start a war. If the Soviet Union can maintain peace and show its construction achievements to the capitalist world, its gains will be many times greater than war. Therefore, if it is not attacked, it will not attack others. However, Japanese warlords are greedy and boastful. After the September 18th Incident, they believe that they have no opponents in the world. Fortunately, their general citizens have long suffered deeply, so the psychology of opposing war is becoming more and more intense. However, they do not dare to speak out, and only express their indignation in indirect ways. Once a war breaks out, assuming that 2 million troops are sent, the daily expenditure will be as high as 40 million yen, and the total monthly expenditure will exceed their annual regular income. Although the ambitions of the Japanese chaebols are great, they must not dare to be reckless. There are still many problems in the northeast, and there are different factions within the military. In the initial stage of the war, they may be able to cope reluctantly. But after a little longer, it will be difficult to predict the outcome. Therefore, the current tense atmosphere between the Sino-Soviet Union is not enough to prove that the two countries will soon go to war.

Tense Sino-Russian Relations

If Russia Does Not Change its Policy Toward Japan 15

Japan Declares it Will Take Necessary Measures

(Tokyo) According to today's Nichinichi Shimbun, Russia has recently taken a series of unfriendly actions towards Japan, which will be a serious warning to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The newspaper predicts that if Russia continues its current policy, Japan will suspend all negotiations with Russia and take the necessary plan to stop its activities. In recent days, officials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of the Army have discussed a strict policy against Russia. The newspaper also listed the unfriendly actions taken by Russia as follows: (1) Russian military aircraft have repeatedly violated the territory of "Manchukuo"; (2) Russian Jiangbin guards have shot at "Manchukuo" ships sailing on the Heilongjiang and Songhua Rivers; (3) Refused the compromise method proposed by Foreign Minister Hirota on the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway; (4) Russian authorities refused to issue passports to fishermen representatives to go to Moscow to participate in the ruble-yen exchange rate negotiations between Russia and Japan. The newspaper also said that the implementation of this policy by the Soviet Union is the result of its recent signing of a non-aggression pact with its western neighbors and reaching an understanding with Eastern European countries. (4th Reuters Telegram)

American Air Force Expansion 16

Army Planes Fly Back from Alaska

One Plane Lands Mid-Journey Due to Lack of Gasoline

(Washington) The U.S. Army Department has now completed its final specific plan for expanding the air force and will submit it to Congress for approval. The plan involves a total expenditure of $3.3 million to purchase anti-aircraft guns, machine guns, and searchlights to be deployed along the coasts and national borders. The important military equipment includes: (1) 3.1-inch anti-aircraft guns with a firing range of 7,500 meters, capable of firing 25 shells per minute; (2) 5-inch machine guns, capable of firing 500 bullets per minute; (3) 800 million candlepower searchlights; (4) construction of power plants; (5) eight regiments of air defense troops, seven regiments of provincial guard troops, and nineteen regiments of reserve troops. Furthermore, the U.S. Air Force plans to purchase 1,000 aircraft, which has been approved by the General Staff. (3rd, Japan Union Telegram)

Ten U.S. Army Department heavy bombers from Angland, Alaska, which had flown in formation from Washington to Alaska last month, began their return journey today. One of the planes, however, suddenly ran out of gasoline mid-flight and was forced to land in a swamp near here. The other nine planes safely arrived here from Wanpunke. The flight crew of the crashed plane were all unharmed, but the plane was completely submerged in mud due to the rising tide and will probably not be able to fly back. The remaining nine planes are expected to arrive in Washington within ten days. (4th, National Telegram)

(Washington) Saturday marked the 144th anniversary of the establishment of the U.S. Coastal Tax Police. Rumors have resurfaced that the force will soon be reorganized by the Navy Department. These rumors circulated widely in Washington several months ago, leading to widespread opposition from those sympathetic to the force. It is claimed that increasing national defense strength and saving expenses are the reasons for the reorganization. At the same time, the Army Department also stated today that it will request appropriations in the next Congress to increase air defense for the United States and the Panama Canal. (3rd, National)

Hundreds of Government Affairs Awaiting Resolution 20

Among those traveling with him will be several cabinet members and members of Congress. Today's drought is increasing the hardship for farmers, and the government's housing program is progressing slowly. Economic recovery has also made little progress during President Roosevelt's vacation. All these issues need President Roosevelt to supervise and promote their implementation. Therefore, the President will face a situation that tests his power after returning to Washington. It is widely believed that the government's new measures have reached the economic class, and while public opinion still supports the general outline of its policies, if the current decline in commerce continues, the opposition to the authorities' policies will inevitably increase. (2nd, Reuters Telegram)

U.S. Naval Base

Overview of Honolulu 21

Japanese-American Citizens are the Most Influential Group on the Island

Annexation to the Federation Will Inevitably Be Realized Sooner or Later

Honolulu Correspondence: President Roosevelt's visit to Honolulu this time, in today's subtle and unpredictable situation in the Far East, is indeed a thought-provoking event. What is the purpose of his visit? Before speculating, let us first look at the history and current situation of Honolulu.

History: Honolulu consists of twenty islands, large and small, of which eleven are uninhabited. It was discovered by Englishman James Cook 156 years ago. For most of the nineteenth century, it maintained its status as the Kingdom of Honolulu. In 1893, it became a republic. In 1900, during President McKinley's era, it was formally annexed to the United States. The total area of all the islands is less than that of Shikoku in Japan. Excluding the uninhabited islands, the total area is 6,454 square miles. According to the 1930 survey, the total population of Honolulu is 368,336 people, and the current estimated number is 380,211 people.

Races: From the perspective of race, the residents of Honolulu include 146,092 Japanese (including 6,461 Koreans), 63,052 Filipinos, 44,895 whites (Americans, British, Germans, and Russians), 28,224 mixed-race people between Hawaiians and other races, 27,588 Portuguese, 27,179 Chinese, 1,219 Spaniards, and 7,351 others.

Although it encompasses such a variety of races, there has never been racial prejudice or conflict, and it is regarded as a peaceful village in the Pacific, known as the birthplace of the Pacific Conference. However, after the incident involving the wife of Lieutenant McIntosh of the Navy in September 1932, in which two Chinese, Filipinos, and Japanese were identified as suspects, a major dispute arose. As a result, the antagonistic relationship between whites and Asian races has also intensified.

Citizens: Honolulu, like Alaska and the Philippines, is different from the states within the United States. It is an external territory of the United States, and its judicial and administrative affairs can be said to be entirely dominated by the governor and judges appointed by the President. However, there is one upper and one lower house. The upper house has fifteen members with a four-year term, and the lower house has thirty members with a two-year term. Currently, there are four Japanese-American citizens as members in the lower house, and there are also Japanese-American citizens as members in the county council. Among the 360,000 residents on the island, about 236,500 have citizenship, including 87,700 Japanese, 42,000 whites, 47,700 Hawaiians and mixed-race people, 15,600 Filipinos, and 15,600 Chinese.

Looking at the table above, Japanese people have the most citizens, accounting for more than one-third, and the trend is increasing. Currently, Honolulu also sends representatives to the U.S. Federal Congress, but they do not have the right to vote. Based on the current situation, it is only a matter of time before Honolulu is established as a state within the United States and its state rights are established. Roosevelt is taking advantage of his visit to Honolulu to conduct on-site investigations into the establishment of state rights, which is a clear fact. Once state rights are established, Honolulu will send one member each to the upper and lower houses of the Federal Congress, and it is not difficult to imagine that Japanese-American citizens will be elected as members at that time. (To be continued)

Poland Leaning Towards Restoring Relations 22

Following Poland's occupation of Vilnius, Lithuania severed diplomatic relations with Poland for twelve years. Polish newspapers have recently predicted that Poland and Lithuania will soon restore diplomatic relations. However, Lithuania is somewhat skeptical about this. According to semi-official sources here, in addition to expressing goodwill to each other, Poland has not yet put forward specific measures for restoring diplomatic relations. Lithuania, on the other hand, is determined not to compromise on the recovery of the lost territory of Vilnius. (3rd, National Telegram)

US-Russia Trade Situation 23

The Benefits Obtained by the United States are Less Than Expected

(Washington) The commercial benefits obtained by the United States in the first half of this year after the United States recognized Soviet Russia are far less than expected. After President Roosevelt met with Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissioner Litvinov last year, the two countries announced the restoration of diplomatic relations. At that time, it was widely believed that Soviet Russia's purchase of American goods would exceed US$100 million. According to statistics released by the Department of Commerce today, American goods imported into Soviet Russia in the first half of this year were worth a total of US$6,417,000, compared with US$2,429,000 in the first half of 1933, and US$74,981,000 in the same period in 1930. Statisticians point out that the devaluation of the gold dollar this year means that the above figures will be even smaller if calculated in Russian currency. To accurately compare this year's exports with last year's, this year's exports should actually be reduced by one-third. Therefore, the actual value of exports in the first half of this year is US$1,848,000. The Soviet Russian side believes that this pessimistic result is due to the obstruction of the Johnson Act. According to the Johnson Act, Soviet Russia, as a country that owes debts to the United States, cannot enjoy the benefits of American public and private loans. It is widely believed here that the settlement of debts may resolve the commercial difficulties between the United States and Russia and revitalize exports to Russia. (3rd, National Telegram)

Inside Story of Hoover's Failure 24

(New York) Former U.S. President Hoover's secretary, Geisling, published an article in Redbook magazine today, stating that the United States never knew about President Hoover's efforts to break the economic panic during his tenure, and said that he had repeatedly advised the President to pay attention to publicity, but the President often said, "I am not an entertainer, I cannot demean my self-worth." He also recalled that Hoover's failure in the second election was due to not being able to defeat Roosevelt's ability to show off. (3rd, National Telegram)

(3rd, National Telegram)

Thousands of British Detectives Mobilized

Red Briefcase Containing Naval Secret Documents 27

A False Alarm: Lost and Found

(London) A red briefcase, containing secret documents of the Navy Department regarding the testing of new guns and new ships, was sent by train from Newcastle to the South. It was suddenly lost between London and Portsmouth. When the authorities heard this news, they were greatly shocked and immediately notified the national police stations to search for it. After a few hours, thousands of people, including amateur detectives and well-known private detective agency personnel, searched for this precious red briefcase. Finally, it was found in Newcastle, the place of origin. Then everyone felt relieved. As for why it was still in the place of origin, it was apparently because the label attached to the briefcase had fallen off, so it was returned to the place of origin. (3rd, Reuters Telegram)

(Berlin) Nazi propaganda expert Goebbels is currently planning a large-scale propaganda campaign for his leader Hitler. Even people in labor camps and detention centers will be escorted by military police to the ballot box to vote. It is expected that the result of this vote will be a large majority for Hitler. At the same time, people across the country are now remotely meditating on the future of the motherland and the domestic and foreign disputes in front of the deceased President's bier. The fate of 65 million Germans is now entirely in Hitler's hands, and their safety cannot be determined quickly. The only thing Hitler uses to overcome these problems is the absolute dictatorial power that is unparalleled in all of Europe. (3rd, Reuters Telegram)

Late German President

Remains Prepared for Burial 32

Loved by the People, Visitors Fill the Door

Funeral Set for Next Tuesday

The ceremony for preparing the remains of President Hindenburg in Neuteck City took place this morning in the President's former office in the villa. Many relatives and guarding officers participated in the ceremony. Some friends from the President's childhood, such as Prince Tauenayishlobyden and Countess Fingenstein, although elderly, came to express their condolences after hearing the news and are expected to arrive here tonight. (4th, Havas Telegram)

(Paris) The funeral date for German President Hindenburg has been set for next Tuesday. President Lebrun has appointed Ambassador Ponce, stationed in Germany, as a special envoy to represent France at the funeral. On that day, all French public institutions in the capital will fly flags at half-mast to express mourning. (4th, Havas Telegram)

(Berlin) Today, people throughout Berlin flocked to the Presidential Palace to pay their respects to the late President, resembling a pilgrimage by religious believers. The signature books prepared in the reception room of the Presidential Palace were signed by millions of people, especially women and young people. Furthermore, the House of Representatives is scheduled to meet on August 6 to commemorate the late President. At that time, Chancellor Hitler will deliver a eulogy, which will be broadcasted to all regions by radio. The Ministry of Education has ordered students from all schools to gather at that time to respectfully listen to the Chancellor's speech. On August 7, the Presidential funeral will be held in front of the Tannenberg Memorial, which will also be broadcasted by radio. All schools will suspend classes to quietly listen. The Nazi Youth League, under the leader's orders, will lay wreaths at the war memorial for the fallen soldiers of the Great War throughout the country on August 7. (3rd, Havas Telegram)

Foreign journalists in Neuteck City were allowed by the authorities to visit the late President's villa this afternoon to pay their respects to General Hindenburg's remains. They first entered the President's mourning hall. The President's remains were lying on the bed, covered with flowers and wreaths, with his hands crossed and his face serene, like sleep. The bed was made of metal and was very simple. A large wreath was placed on the bed, and four officers of the National Defense Force stood guard with swords on both sides. The remains were covered with a white felt cloth, on which was placed a bullet, because when Hindenburg was a lieutenant colonel, two bullets passed over his head during the Battle of Sadowa, and this was one of them. The foreign reporters then entered the President's former office, where a large portrait of the President's entire body was hung. There was also a glass cabinet displaying many trophies, all obtained by Hindenburg during the Battle of Sadowa when he was a lieutenant colonel. In his library, the walls were covered with honorary degrees, honorary citizen certificates, and doctoral diplomas that the President had received during his lifetime. The honorary sword hanging on the wall was given by the Japanese government after the Great War to praise the General's Bushido spirit. The dining room contained fine porcelain made by the French Sèvres factory, which was given by the German government on the President's 85th birthday. Finally, the reporters toured the gardens near the villa, where the President often strolled in the evenings. His ancestral tomb was also selected to be buried here. (3rd, Havas Telegram)

President's Will

Searched Everywhere Without Success 33

(Berlin) A surprising piece of news was spread in Berlin today, stating that the late President Hindenburg's last will and testament could not be found. Mr. Meisner, Hindenburg's secretary, searched for this document in the Presidential Palace in Berlin without success, and it was also not found in the Neuteck villa. Many believe that the issue of the late President's burial place has not been definitively decided, probably because the will has not been found. (4th, Reuters Telegram)

Where to Return the Bones

Not Yet Decided 34

(Berlin) According to reports from some people, it seems that the burial of the late President Hindenburg in the Tannenberg Memorial has not been permitted by his family, because Hindenburg's last wish was only to be buried in his ancestral tomb in Neuteck City. Therefore, it is also possible that only a funeral will be held in Tannenberg on Tuesday, without burial there. (3rd, Havas Telegram)

(Berlin) When the remains of the late President Hindenburg are held in a state funeral at the Tannenberg Memorial at 11:00 a.m. next Tuesday, the surviving soldiers who participated in the Battle of Tannenberg will be transported by special train from various places to participate in the late Field Marshal's last honors to commemorate the Battle of Tannenberg. (3rd, National Telegram)

(Berlin) Tannenberg is a vast plain with rivers and lakes separating it. There are eight square towers standing around, surrounded by city walls, resembling a fortress from the feudal era. This is the victory memorial for the late General Hindenburg. In August 1914, Hindenburg defeated the Russian army here, recovered lost territory, and rose to fame in one fell swoop. Afterwards, a monument was built to commemorate his achievements. Not far from the village, there is a small marble monument, which is a memorial to another Battle of Tannenberg in 1410, when Prussian King Magellan led a large army to fight and defeat the Teutonic Knights, establishing suzerainty. Therefore, Tannenberg is a historical memorial site in Germany. Now, General Hindenburg is buried here, and in front of his tomb is the battlefield where blood was shed in 1914, with countless crosses and tens of thousands of skeletons buried beneath it. (3rd, Havas Telegram)

(Beiping) Bao Yueqing said, "I came to Beiping on the orders of Prince Yun, along with Guo Wang, as representatives to urge He Yingqin to quickly assume the position of Director of Guidance for Mongolian Autonomy. We will immediately visit the Panchen Lama and He Yingqin to establish a public office. The Mongolian local administrative plan has already been approved by the Central Government, but since the Director of Guidance has not yet taken office, all facilities have not yet been prepared or implemented. The Mongolian Political Council's expenses have been approved by the Central Government at 30,000 yuan per month, but since it still needs to be audited, it has not yet been allocated. We can temporarily borrow from the Ministry of Finance. Prince De and Prince Yun are both working at the council's office. Since the council's office was moved out of Bailingmiao, it is now operating in nearby Mongolian yurts. The guards live in tents. The issue of building a new office has been addressed, and several sites have been selected within ten li around Bailingmiao, but in accordance with religious regulations, it must be designated by the Panchen Lama before a decision can be made. We plan to submit a budget to the Central Government to allocate construction funds. The twelve banners of Chahar have officially reorganized into a league, with the Central Government passing the eight principles of Mongolian autonomy. The Central Government's official order has not yet arrived. The former Security Chief and Lieutenant General Zhuo Tu Bajia Bu has been elected as the league leader, and Fu Ling'a is the deputy league leader. The wireless telegraph machine issued by the Central Government will be transported to Bailingmiao within days and distributed to the banners for use." (4th Special Telegram)

Jiaoji Railway Train Collision 47

(Qingdao) At 7:00 AM on the 4th, the Jiaoji Railway westbound No. 51 passenger train was traveling to Tabao Station when the eastbound No. 102 freight train's air brake failed. Unable to stop, it directly collided with the passenger train. As a result, three sections of the track were damaged, and the passenger train's locomotive was derailed. Only the first two cars of the freight train's locomotive were derailed. One stoker had his leg broken, and one passenger was slightly injured. Fortunately, the rest were unharmed. Upon receiving the report, the railway bureau immediately dispatched the directors of the engineering, transportation, and locomotive departments, along with cadres and 50 workers, on a special train at 12:00 PM to provide assistance, bringing a 30-ton crane. As of yet, it has not been repaired. The temporary workaround for eastbound and westbound passenger trains is for passengers to disembark at the accident site and transfer to the other train, then each train returns to allow travel. However, freight trains have been temporarily suspended. As of the time of the telegram, it has not yet been repaired. (4th Special Telegram)

(Jinan) At 10:30 this morning, the Jiaoji Railway No. 51 passenger train collided with a freight train at Tabao Station, with minor losses. (4th Special Telegram)

Jiangnan Long-Distance Bus Robbery Case

Three Robbers Arrested 49

(Nanjing) On the 25th of last month, a Jiangnan long-distance bus traveling from Changxing to Nanjing was robbed by four bandits when it reached the Xicun Station area near Maqun Town in Jiangning County. The bandits escaped without a trace after the incident. The Capital Police Department, upon receiving the report, believed that although the incident occurred within the jurisdiction of Jiangning County, it was adjacent to the city and had a significant impact on the security of the capital. They ordered strict investigation and surveillance. It was soon discovered that the case was committed by bandits Ding Litian, Sun Huailin, Zhu San, and Liu Huatang, and that Jin Xiangwen, of No. 26 Qianmen Street, Puzhen, Jiangpu County, was harboring them. The police managed to arrest Ding Litian and two other bandits. Liu Huatang escaped elsewhere and has not been apprehended. At the same time, two Mauser pistols, one handgun, one Mauser rifle, and seven swords were found at Jin Xiangwen's home. Jin Xiangwen fled upon hearing the news. After the bandits were arrested and brought to the police department, they all confessed to the robbery. The evidence and other items have been handed over to the Nanjing Garrison Headquarters for review and handling. (4th Special Telegram)

Regulations on Marriage and Funeral Rites 50

Ministry of Communications Utilizes Aviation

To Deliver International Mail 51

(Nanjing) Communications circles report that before the September 18th Incident, China's international mail was delivered to Europe via the Siberian Railway, which was relatively convenient in terms of time. After the Northeast fell, the route was blocked and changed to be delivered to Europe via the Suez Canal, which took a little longer. Recently, after detailed research and improvement by the Directorate General of Posts of the Ministry of Communications, it was decided to utilize the Royal Airmail line between London and Singapore to transport international mail, which is faster in terms of time. After contacting the Royal Shipping Company, the plan was submitted to the Ministry for review. The Ministry believes that the method is feasible and has ordered the Directorate General of Posts to instruct postal bureaus in various districts to comply. (4th Special Telegram)

Qiantang River Bridge Construction

Construction Expected to Start Next Month 52

(Hangzhou) The Ministry and the Province are cooperating to build the Qiantang River Bridge. Huang Boqiao was sent by the Ministry of Railways to Hangzhou as a representative to discuss cooperation methods with Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Construction Department. The results were satisfactory. Huang immediately went to Shanghai and then to Beijing to report back. The agreed content of cooperation is as follows: (1) The cost of the bridge project is 5 million yuan, with the Ministry and the Province each bearing 2.5 million yuan. (2) Both parties will jointly form a bridge engineering committee to plan all matters, with each party having half of the committee members. (3) No separate engineering office will be established; the existing engineering office will handle the matter. (4) Bidding will be approved on August 22nd, and construction will officially begin in September. (4th Special Telegram)

Price of Rice and Flour Soars in Tianjin 58

The reason for the fall is the large-scale import of leftover copper coins from the puppet state through Shanhaiguan and transported to Tianjin. He only managed to avoid losing Hebei amidst popular panic. Now that the overall situation has been settled and the situation has changed, we must provide relief to the people and restore their vitality, and we must also invigorate our spirits and move forward with great determination to rectify politics and military affairs. Anyone who is perfunctory or follows the old ways will not be tolerated. From now on, we should strive to practice four things: (1) being punctual; (2) using domestic goods; (3) abstaining from smoking and gambling; and (4) being peaceful in attitude, in order to comply with the spirit of the New Life Movement. International Commercial Telegraph 74

丨Reuter's Special Commercial News from London, August 4th丨

Gold and Silver

London gold price fell one penny today to 138 shillings and a halfpenny.

London Silver Market: London silver market prices rose due to buying from the United States, India, and China. Spot price is 20 pence 6875, up 1875; futures price is 20 pence 8125, up 25. China later switched from buying to selling.

Securities

Before the opening of the New York stock market, factors favorable to the market situation were: (1) improved trading, hoping to curb buying sprees, but this factor lacked activity; (2) the possibility of General Motors issuing an extra dividend, which is still under discussion; (3) widespread belief that President Roosevelt will soon issue statements to stabilize general trade. Factors unfavorable to the market situation were: (1) unstable markets for all major commodities; (2) railway freight loading figures are unusually low for this time of year. This morning in the stock exchange, talk of inflation seemed to be cooling down. The dollar is relatively stable. Securities opened weakly and steadily with balanced buying and selling. It is expected that price fluctuations will remain small and insignificant.

Exchange Rates

The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The opening exchange rate between British and American currencies was the same as yesterday's closing rate. At 11:00 AM, it rose by one eight seven five, to five dollars four cents five six two five. At 1:00 PM, it fell by three one two five, to five dollars four cents two five. One US dollar equals three shillings eleven pence five nine five in British currency.

The foreign exchange market between the US and UK was quiet today. The exchange rate between the US and UK opened at five dollars four cents two five. It rose slightly before noon, to five dollars four cents three seven five. The price remained unchanged at 11:00 AM.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: The New York cotton market was relatively loose, and prices were slightly lower. Southern suppliers and individual investors sold off small amounts.

New York Wheat: Wheat opened quietly, then steadily and firmly, but the opening price this morning showed little change.

Liverpool Wheat: Liverpool wheat market prices rose today. At 1:00 PM, the October futures price was six shillings and one penny and seventy-five, up one penny six two five.

Public and Private Construction Matters

Will Be Managed by an Internal Department 76

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan convened its subordinate ministries and commissions on the 4th to review the proposal to establish an agency in charge of public and private construction matters. As a result, in order to save public funds, it was decided not to establish a separate agency. It was decided to amend the Organic Law of the Ministry of Interior, adding one or two sections to the Department of Civil Affairs or the Department of Land of the Ministry of Interior to manage all public and private construction, as well as planning and review matters. The matter will be submitted to the Yuan meeting for discussion after the preparations are completed (Special dispatch on the 4th).

Henan Provincial Government Passes

Rules for Implementing Joint Office Work 80

(Kaifeng) On the 4th, the Provincial Government meeting passed the draft rules for implementing joint office work. First, the Civil Affairs and Education Departments and the Secretariat and Security Office will be concentrated. The rest will be incorporated successively after the public office is expanded. Each department will have three or four sections, the Secretariat will have three sections and four offices, and the Security Office will have two sections and one unit. The heads of each department and office may issue department or office orders for the conduct of affairs of their respective subordinate agencies, within the scope of not conflicting with the orders of the central government and the province. In addition, all documents of the entire government will be received and sent by the Secretariat, and then distributed to the relevant departments and offices for handling, writing, proofreading, and managing files. The Secretariat will manage them centrally. All drafts of the entire government, except for department or office orders, which will be judged by the heads of the respective departments and offices, will be submitted by the respective departments and offices to the Secretary-General for review and then to the Chairman for judgment. When writing, the heads of the respective departments and offices will countersign. It will be implemented after being approved by the Xingying and filed with the Executive Yuan (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th).

Anhui Provincial Government

All Committee Members Survey Disaster 84

Liu Zhenhua and Others Go to the Lower Reaches of Various Counties

Ma Lingfu and Others Go to the Upper Reaches of Various Counties

Anqing dispatch, since the beginning of summer this year, Anhui Province has been suffering from a long drought, and disaster has already formed along the river. The provincial government specially convened a temporary meeting of all provincial committee members at 6:00 PM on the 30th to decide to carry out drought relief work starting from the 31st. The chairman and all provincial committee members will personally go to more than ten counties along the river to investigate. Where there are dikes and sluices, permission will be given to open the sluices to irrigate fields if there is no danger of flooding. Therefore, after the regular meeting of the provincial government adjourned at 8:30 AM on the 31st, everyone set off in two teams. Provincial Government Chairman Liu Zhenhua, Provincial Party Affairs Special Commissioner Miao Peicheng, Education Director Yang Lian, Tongcheng County Magistrate Yu Yuying, and Engineer Fan Jiagan of the Water Conservancy Engineering Office took the Anfeng ferry to the lower reaches of various counties. Civil Affairs Director Ma Lingfu, Construction Director Liu Yiyan, Huaining County Magistrate Sun Peifang, Jiang Shihui, the first section chief of the Construction Department, and Xu Hansan, the eighth director of the Provincial Government Secretariat, took the Anzhen ferry to the upper reaches of various counties to inspect the drought prevention situation in their respective counties.

The provincial government has repeatedly received reports from various counties on the recent drought situation. The following is a record: (1) Huaining: No rain in the four borders, drought has appeared. The ponds and dams in the high-lying areas of the third, fourth, and fifth districts have dried up, and the seedlings have withered. Although water is drawn with difficulty in low-lying fields near the water, if it does not rain for several more days, the water source will also dry up. (2) Susong: Since the rain on June 28, it has been a month, and the seedlings have felt the drought. The newly built ponds and dams are mostly dry. (3) Wangjiang: There has been no rain for a long time, the ponds and dams are dry, and the seedlings have all withered. If it does not rain for a few more days, the disaster will be extremely serious. (4) Tongcheng: There has been no drop of rain for more than forty days, and the ponds built last year have been exhausted. (5) Dangtu: Mountain fields account for three-tenths, and most of the mountain fields have not been planted. Rain only started on July 20 and 21. (6) Wuhu: There has been no rain for a long time, and the entire territory is a polder village, so water can still be drawn for irrigation. However, the labor costs are too great in extremely high areas, and even if there is a harvest, it will not be worth the loss. Rain only started on July 20 and 21. (7) Fanchang: Mountain fields account for three-tenths. The bottom water of the newly built ponds and dams has been exhausted for a long time due to the drought. Villages with tides can only take care of the present, and about five-sixths of the area is affected by the drought. (8) Guichi: The drought-affected fields in each district account for about 70%. Although there has been rain in the entire territory, it has not penetrated. (9) Tongling: Two weeks of drought, seedlings withered. It rained on July 22, and the seedlings recovered slightly. (10) Wuwei: Mountain fields account for three-tenths, and polder fields account for seven-tenths. The mountain fields have all been affected by the drought. It rained on July 17. (11) Dingyuan: The areas most affected by the drought are the first, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts. Not only has the rice not been planted, but also beans and other items have not been planted, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. (12) Mengcheng: Although it has rained, it is still dry within thirty miles of the city. (13) Huoqiu: No rain for more than twenty days, and the disaster situation is quite serious. (14) Jiashan: The county is entirely an Okada, and the ponds and dams have long been exhausted. Not only has the body not been planted, but also miscellaneous grains have mostly withered. (15) Shexian: There are some signs of drought, and preparations are being made for prevention. (16) Xixi: No rain for fifty days, and all ponds and dams are now releasing water. (17) Ningguo: The weather is dry, and there are many places lacking water. (18) Jingxian: No rain for fifty days, and high and low fields have become scorched earth. (19) Jingde: Except for the third district, which rained on July 10, the rest are dry. (20) Hefei: Dry land is affected by drought, and polder fields can be harvested. (21) Chaoxian: No rain for more than a month, and drought has formed. Although there was a shower on July 16, it was of no help. (22) Lujiang: Okada is affected by drought. Although it has rained recently, it is not universal. (23) Chuxian: The county has 400,000 mu. If it rains before the beginning of autumn, 300,000 mu of drought-resistant crops can still be replanted. (24) Lai'an: The drought situation has formed, and there is no way to remedy it. If there is heavy rain in the next few days, it is still possible to replant mung beans and buckwheat. (25) Quanjiao: The high Okada land accounts for more than twice the amount of polder land, and all the transplanted seedlings have withered. (26) Xuancheng: There are slight signs of drought, but there was a through rain on July 21. (27) Guangde: No rain for two months, and the wasteland has formed. (28) Langxi: A long drought has caused a disaster, but it rained on July 20. (29) Taihu: High-lying areas have slightly become drought-stricken, and places near the river can still be irrigated. If there is heavy rain in three or four days, the loss will not be great. Other counties have turned from severe to light due to receiving through rain, and some have suddenly reported drought due to prolonged sunny weather. If it still does not rain for a long time, the drought will inevitably spread further (2nd).

Wuhu dispatch, Provincial Government Chairman Liu Zhenhua, Education Director Yang Lian, Provincial Party Affairs Special Commissioner Miao Peicheng, Provincial Government Secretary Cao Shaoying, and others took the Anfeng ferry from Anqing to Guangfengwei and Saozhougou in Dongliu County, and then inspected the disaster situation all the way through Datong in Tongling County, Liujadu in Wuwei County, and Digang in Fanchang County. They arrived at Wubu at 9:50 last night (1st). The heads of various agencies, leaders of gentry and business circles, and military police all welcomed them on the riverbank. After Liu and others landed, they went to the Southeast Hotel to meet with representatives from all walks of life. According to the talks, the drought situation witnessed in various places is rare in recent years. In the past, due to major flood disasters, only flood prevention was initially emphasized. Now that the drought situation has formed and there is a lack of sufficient drought relief equipment, now they can only relieve one point of drought, that is, reduce one point of suffering for the people. The matter is also urgent, so the way to provide emergency relief is to first consider the situation and persuade farmers to open the sluices to save the majority of farmland, because opening the sluices is not a major obstacle and can be closed immediately. Liu and others stayed for only two hours and then boarded the ship again, and set sail for He County at dawn this morning. After inspecting He County, they will go to Dangtu, and will return to Wuhu from Dangtu tonight to return to Anqing, planning to take another road to inspect the inland of southern Anhui (2nd).

The Western Route Army Captured

The Pseudo Division Commander Yu Xingzhou 85

Has Been Escorted from Xiushui to Pingxiang

Important Bandit Xin Keming Was Also Captured

Pingxiang Newsletter: Yu Xingzhou, the commander of the Pseudo Independent 1st Division, who has wreaked havoc in northwestern Jiangxi for years, was captured alive by the Yue Sen Department of the 50th Division in Xiushui on July 10. After being reported, Liu Yinggu, commander of the Western Route Column, immediately telegraphed and ordered troops to escort him to the headquarters for interrogation. He was then escorted to the headquarters by a company of the 50th Division on the 26th. The details are as follows:

Arrival at Headquarters: The people of Pingxiang, hearing that the bandit leader Yu had been captured, rushed to see him. When the escorted bandit Yu arrived in the county, the people rushed to see him, vying to be the first. For a time, the entrance to the headquarters of the longitudinal tunnel was full of people, blocking the road.

Yu Bandit's Background: Yu Bandit is from Xie in Pingjiang, Hunan. He is 26 years old this year. He is small, fierce, and brave, with bright eyes. Although his face is dark and his hair is disheveled, he shows no fear. He worked as a farmhand for two years, and then made a living as a boatman with his father. He also served as a soldier in the 2nd Battalion of the 7th Regiment of the 3rd Division of the 35th Army for two years. His father still works as a boatman. He has a wife at home.

Experiences as a Bandit: In 1928, Yu Bandit served as a township farmer in Pingjiang and participated in the Red Bandit Riot. In 1929, he joined the Communist Party through Gao Yongsheng and served as the captain of the Pingjiang Guerrilla. In 1930, he served as the captain of the Red Guards when attacking Changsha. In 1931, he served as the battalion commander of the Red Police Guard Battalion of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Province. In the winter of 1932, he served as the commander of the Independent Regiment of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Military Region and a member of the Standing Committee of the Communist Party of China in Xiutong Yifeng. In the spring of 1933, he served as a member of the Second Executive Committee of the Soviet of Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Province and as the Minister of Military Affairs of Xiutong Yifeng. In August of the same year, he was transferred to serve as the commander of the Independent 1st Division of the Red Army of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Military Bandits. On October 15, he was elected as an executive committee member at the Third Congress of Workers, Peasants, and Soldiers of the Pseudo-Provincial Soviet. Last autumn, he was repeatedly suppressed by the regiment, and his strength suffered losses. In February of this year, he was reorganized into the 4th Independent Regiment of the Red Army of Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Province, and he was reassigned as the regiment commander. Over the years, he has fought against the National Army hundreds of times, used guns hundreds of times, and been wounded three times. He has worked the longest and hardest in Yifeng, Xiushui, Tonggu, Fengxin, Gao'an, and other counties.

Special Talents in Life: Yu Bandit is physically strong and capable of wrestling with tigers. He is good at boxing and swimming. In peacetime, even a dozen people could not compete with him in combat. His fierce and domineering nature is his nature.

Twice Received Special Awards: In addition to having a wife in his old home in Pingjiang, he was introduced to Tang Yu, a graduate of the Red Army School and Minister of Women in Yifeng County, by the Marriage Department of the Provincial Soviet in 1929. Last year, during the Battle of Huangsha, Tang was captured by the 77th Division in Xiaoyao. In February of this year, he cohabited with Chen Ying, who is from Liuyang and a middle school student, through the introduction of the Provincial Soviet. She studied at the Red Army School, likes military affairs, and can also fight. The marriage certificate will be officially issued after the school's trial period is over (according to bandits' marriages, there is no ceremony, and the marriage is established when the County Soviet or Provincial Soviet issues a marriage certificate). Unexpectedly, the net of heaven is vast, and the good dream has not yet come true before he was captured.

Details of Capture: Since Liu Yinggu was stationed in western Jiangxi to suppress the bandits, he has repeatedly made outstanding achievements. Before and after the head of the bandit Gao Yongsheng was surrendered, countless bandit leaders were captured and surrendered. In April of this year, he ordered Yue Division to find a way to recruit Yu Bandit, but it was unsuccessful. Unexpectedly, on July 10, Yu Bandit led his troops to occupy the Shelinkeng area of Huangshagang in Xiushui. After being secretly reported, the 3rd Battalion of the 299th Regiment of the Yue Division pursued and suppressed him on the 13th. The bandits had already been defeated. The bandit led his troops to live in seclusion on Huangshagang Ridge. The ridge stretches for more than a hundred miles and is dangerous with forty-eight water gullies. The battalion searched on the ridge for a day and a night before discovering it in a cave. At that time, the bandit still had more than 20 guards who resisted stubbornly. After a lot of hand-to-hand combat, all of them were disarmed and Yu Bandit Xingzhou and five other traffic officers, Yang Yongbiao, were captured together. After being identified by a surrendered person, they were escorted back to the headquarters and reported to the superiors.

Pre-Trial Interview: The reporter once spoke with Yu Bandit. The reporter asked, "Why do you want to be a bandit and do evil?" Yu Bandit replied, "I have not studied and do not understand politics. My actions are completely commanded by the political commissar. Now that I have been captured here, I know that this is the road to light." Asked, "When did you become a division commander?" Replied, "I became a division commander step by step. The Communist Party of China is usually very satisfied with me. They have repeatedly sent political personnel to talk to me, probably because they think I have three advantages. One is the farmhand class, two is a few years of fighting history, and three is firm political belief. But I believe that charging into battle is my strength, and I am sure of leading troops, which is my ability." When he spoke, he often smiled fiercely, as if he had little intention of repentance.

Pseudo Division Commander Yu Xingzhou

Overview of the Trial: On the morning of the 27th, Liu Yinggu ordered Chief of Staff Guo, together with Judge Chen, to open a court to try Yu Bandit. At 6:00 PM, Liu personally appeared in court for review and invited Xu Zhigan, Chief of the Staff Office of the Western Route Headquarters, Li Bofen, Acting Chief of the Military Law Office, Wang Bangshu, Liaison Staff Officer of the Xingying, Wei Suzhou, Administrative Commissioner of the Second District, and Liu Xuehao, former Director of the Political Department of the Pseudo-Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Military Region who was appointed as a colonel after surrendering, to attend the trial. Record Secretary Li Zengyu instructed Yu Bandit to state his experiences as a bandit in court. Yu confessed without concealment. The most important thing was that Commander Liu asked, "Why didn't you surrender earlier? Have you not seen the leaflets distributed by our headquarters welcoming your surrender?" Yu replied, "I don't know. Because I am illiterate, I don't know how to surrender." He also asked, "How many guerrillas are there still in the northwestern Jiangxi area?" Yu replied, "There are six more, with a total of more than a hundred guns. Many have been seized. There is one in each of Tianbao, Xiaoyao, Dongzhuang, Ganfang, Huangsha, and Shixi." He also asked, "Why was Kong Hechong transferred to a pseudo-central position?" Yu replied, "The central government said that he was impractical and that he had suffered too many losses." He also asked, "How many guns does your own unit still have?" Yu replied, "There are still about a hundred guns." He also asked, "How many guns does Xu Bandit Yangang have?" Yu replied, "The original department had only dozens of guns after being reorganized into the 46th Regiment. Recently, they have been repeatedly surrounded and seized by the National Army. Each gun has only one row of bullets. It is heard that Xu has fled to Jingbei with dozens of people." The interrogation lasted for three hours before the court was adjourned. Yu Bandit was still taken back into custody. After a short rest, Xin Keming, the Provincial Committee Member of the Pseudo-Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi District and Minister of White District Work, was brought in for interrogation.

Request for Instructions on Handling: Commander Liu telegraphed to the Western Route Headquarters yesterday, saying, "Commander He of Changsha General Headquarters, according to the report of Division Commander Yue, captured the pseudo-division commander Yu Xingzhou alive and the report of Division Commander Zhu captured the pseudo-provincial committee member Xin Keming alive. They have arrived at the headquarters one after another. I personally appeared in court and invited Liaison Staff Officer Wang of the Xingying, Director Xu of the Headquarters, Military Law Officer Li, Liu Xuehao, Advisor, Commissioner Wei, and others to attend the joint trial and interrogation. According to Yu Xingzhou's confession, he served as platoon leader, squad leader, company battalion commander, commander of the Independent 4th Regiment, commander of the Independent 1st Division, and a member of the Executive Committee of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Soviet, Minister of Military Affairs of Xiutong Yifeng, and other important pseudo-positions. Xin Keming confessed that he had served as a member of the Standing Committee of the Pseudo-Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Soviet and served as the Minister of Security Zone Work, and White Zone Inspector. Each directly admitted without concealment, and Liu Xuehao, Advisor, proved in court that he knew the two bandits and that they were indeed the same people and had held important positions. In particular, Yu Bandit Xingzhou was fierce and good at fighting and was a contemporary figure of Kong Bandit Hechong, who was always valued by Kong Bandit. After investigation, Yu Xingzhou and Xin Keming are both important members of the bandits. After repeated inquiries, their confessions have been recorded in the file. In addition to submitting a copy of the confession, I would like to ask whether the two bandits should be escorted to Changsha to await your interrogation, or whether they should be tried near Pingxiang by your department. I am awaiting your telegraphic instructions, Liu Yinggu." (July 28)

Wuhu Rice Prices Continue to Soar 86

丨Various Counties Request to Open Sluices for Water Diversion丨

Wuhu Dispatch, the drought in Anhui Province is almost all over the province. Although there were slight showers a few days ago, the farmland benefited very little. Recently, it has still been abnormally early, with an average temperature of more than 1023 degrees, which is very hot. The upper reaches of Tongling, Chaoxian, Tongcheng, and other places are particularly severely affected, and food and water are difficult to maintain. Rice grains are no longer transported. To prevent food shortages among the people, they have all come to Wuhu to purchase large quantities of rice from various rice mills and transport them to Datong and other places. In a few days, the price of rice, which was six yuan per stone, has soared to nine yuan and several jiao, and there is still a tendency to continue to rise. It is now found that the market price of rice from the upper machine is nine yuan and three jiao per stone, the secondary machine is eight yuan and seven jiao, and the second time is seven yuan and six or seven jiao. Wheat and other miscellaneous grains are also firm and popular. Jin and Hu and other places have sent personnel to stay and let go of procurement. There are three to four thousand stones traded every day. Shangzhou wheat is currently sold for three taels and eight qian per stone, ordinary three taels and six qian, and three taels and two or three qian. The reason why rice prices are soaring is that the mainland is preventing famine and the source is not surging. However, the transaction of large-scale rice businesses between Guang and Chao gangs is still stagnant, because the sound of ordering foreign rice is very loud, and Annan rice takes the opportunity to sell cheaply in southern China.

Various counties have reported to the provincial government on the serious drought and requested to open the sluices for water diversion. The Construction Department has already formulated six measures for opening the sluices to prevent drought and has telegraphed them to various counties for strict compliance: (1) If the villagers request to open the dikes for water diversion due to force majeure, the inner dikes should be reported to the local water conservancy branch for approval, and the Jiang dikes should be reported to the county magistrate and the stationed dike committee for joint inspection and approval, and sufficient soil and pile materials should be prepared to ensure that they can be rushed to build at any time before they can be opened according to the instructions; (2) A guarantee shall be provided for requesting the opening of a dike to be responsible for its protection and repair. The guarantee period shall be until the end of September next year; (3) The length of the dike that may be opened shall be limited to the date of blocking and building, and shall be carefully verified by the person in charge of approval; (4) The person in charge of approval shall indicate the location of the dike to be opened to avoid any danger; (5) The person in charge of approval shall prepare a report on the location, shape, and length of the dike to be opened, together with the guarantee provided by the villagers, and send it to the county government in time to be classified and recorded in a special register, and registered and stored separately, and reported immediately after the blocking is completed and the verification is solid for registration and investigation; (6) The county government shall report the location, shape, and length of the dike opened to the Construction Department at any time according to the report, so as to pay special attention to it during flood prevention. This also implies the meaning of prevention in the midst of drought relief. (2nd)

Jintan District Chiefs

Request for Demolition of the Fragrant Grass River Dam Foundation 87

To Chairman Chen of the Jiangsu Provincial Government: The cunning people of Danyang, including Ma Xiting (also known as Ma Qipei and Ma Xiting), are malicious and disregard the law and reason. During this time of severe drought, they built a dam on the Fragrant Grass River in the Jiuli area of the county, cutting off the public water supply downstream. The affected people have repeatedly elected representatives to petition the provincial government and various legal organizations to appeal. The dam has not yet been opened, and the suffering downstream is evident. Considering only Jintan County, not only is there no water to irrigate the farmland, but drinking water has also dried up. The lives of hundreds of thousands of people in the county are in imminent danger. Therefore, it is necessary to truthfully and tearfully explain the relationship of the river, the reason for building the dam, the situation of the suffering, the comparison of gains and losses, and the excuses of the culprits to your Excellency, the Chairman. First, the river meanders for hundreds of miles, and each county calls it by different names. In Danyang, it is called the Fragrant Grass River, in Jintan, it is called the Taiping River, and in Liyang and Yixing, it is called the Li Canal. The water flows in from the Yangtze River, passes through the southern countryside of Danyang and Zhenjiang counties, enters the western countryside of Jintan, passes through the eastern countryside, and finally reaches the lakeside of Liyang and Yixing. Furthermore, in the middle reaches of Tan County, it branches out like blood vessels, running through the entire county. Since the beginning of civilization, people have relied on this river as a source of irrigation for farmland and drinking water. In addition, the transportation of agricultural products, fertilizers, and seeds cannot be done without this river. This is the first thing to note regarding the importance of this river. Second, in Danyang, the upstream area, the fields are low and the river is high, while in Jintan and other downstream counties, the river is low and the fields are high. It is very easy to draw water upstream, but very difficult downstream. The cunning people, Ma Xiting, and others took advantage of this situation and suddenly built two dams, an upper and a lower dam, in the vicinity of Zini Han and the old county in Jiuli Town, Danyang County, in the second ten days of July. This severely blocked the water, allowing not a single drop to flow through. When the tide comes from the river, it can directly flow into the fields without the need for machinery or labor, thus achieving natural irrigation. The rent for the fields will be doubled, and the tenants will reap the benefits without labor. They believe that the construction of the dam is a clever feat of nature. The lower dam in the old county controls more than 1,000 acres of land, and the upper dam in Zini Han controls more than 20,000 acres of land, which are cultivated by the people living at the intersection of the three counties of Danyang, Zhenjiang, and Jintan. Ma Xiting and others deceived the provincial government and claimed that it was done by the people of several counties, but in reality, it was a small number of people seeking personal gain at the expense of the public. This is the second thing to note regarding the reason for building the dam. Third, since the two dams were built in the second ten days of July, the western countryside of Jintan was the first to suffer. In towns such as Shima Bridge, Xiyang, Qingfu, and Hezhixi Bridge, the lack of water to irrigate and save the farmland is already a tragic sight. Moreover, tens of thousands of residents are suffering from a lack of drinking water in this sweltering heat. To obtain half a bucket of muddy water, they must fetch it from more than ten miles away, resulting in widespread epidemics and countless deaths. Now, the rivers in the eastern, southern, and northern countryside have been successively cut off, and the severity of the disaster is unprecedented. All the fields in Jintan's countryside have access to rivers, and the riverbed is lower than the river flow, with the waterline being about ten feet. If the upstream dam had not blocked the source, no matter how severe the drought, there would be no reason for a lack of irrigation water. According to statistics, the farmland in the county that relies on river tides for irrigation is more than 700,000 acres. Now that the water source has been suddenly cut off, the loss per acre is calculated at ten yuan, amounting to more than seven million yuan. Furthermore, people are dying due to the lack of drinking water. The misery of the situation is beyond words. This is the third thing to note regarding the situation of the suffering. Fourth, the river water flows from the Yangtze River day and night, and of course, it is inexhaustible. If it is said that the river is low downstream and the water flows rapidly downwards, and the upstream will soon dry up, it should be known that according to the principles of water, the downstream flows out rapidly, and the upstream estuary naturally and rapidly flows in, without a moment's pause. This principle is very clear. Ma Xiting and others lack scientific knowledge and morality, so they have lost their conscience and dare to do what is wrong. The distance between the fields in these two places and the water surface is only one or two feet. If a public water-lifting machine is installed, the cost will be at most 7,000 yuan. If manual labor is used instead of a machine, it is already vastly different from the downstream, where cars are set up layer upon layer in high fields. However, in order to save the cost of 7,000 yuan, they disregarded the loss of more than seven million yuan downstream. A small number of people upstream are lazy, steal time, and sit and reap the benefits, while hundreds of thousands of people downstream are trapped in a dry ditch and cannot even save their lives. This is the fourth thing to note regarding the comparison of gains and losses. Fifth, the culprits who built the dam, including Ma Qipei, Chen Suigeng, Ouyang Hao, Wang Mingda, Li Daonan, Wei Xingguo, and Geng Hai'ao, actually petitioned the provincial government to protect the dam, claiming that the river was dredged by the people of Danyang and that the dam has a historical connection. In fact, this is completely unfounded and self-deceptive. The river stretches for hundreds of miles, from Zhenjiang and Danyang to Jintan, Liyang, and Yixing, and flows into the lake. It is a public river, so how can it be separated by a ditch? Furthermore, the riverbed at that location is shallow and narrow, while from Jintan downwards, it is deep and substantial. It is easy to access the river tide, and the water volume is sufficient. The fact that it has not been dredged for many years is already evident. As for the history of dam construction, according to the inscriptions at the site, during the Chongzhen period of the Ming Dynasty, Li Jiwen built a dam in the old county area, and the Zhenjiang prefectural government punished him with caning and erected a stone tablet to prohibit it forever. This is enough to prove that dam construction in that area is prohibited. Recently, in the eleventh year of the Republic of China, Zhou Juntang and others built a dam at the Dongxi River head and were sentenced to imprisonment. In the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, Governor Han Guojun and Military Governor Qi Xieyuan jointly issued a proclamation forever prohibiting the construction of dams in the Xiangcao River area. The representatives have presented it to the Civil Affairs Department for review. Now, the Republic of China has not changed, and the river has not changed either. How can right and wrong be reversed, and the consequence be turned into the cause? This is the fifth thing to note regarding the excuses and deceptions of the culprits. Ma Xiting and others deceive the government above and harm neighboring counties below. Now, hundreds of thousands of people downstream are barely breathing. Therefore, we urgently submit this petition, earnestly requesting the provincial government to quickly dispatch public security troops to demolish the dam foundation and send water police to station there for defense. We anxiously await your orders. Tu Yu, Standing Committee Member of the Jintan County Party Executive Committee, Bao Kan, Chief of the Jintan County Farmers' Association, Ma Yintang, Chairman of the Jintan County Chamber of Commerce, Tu Ding, District Chief of the First District, Sun Jiangzuo, District Chief of the Second District, Zhang Quan, District Chief of the Third District, Li Rui, District Chief of the Fourth District, Ling Zilian, District Chief of the Fifth District, and Yu Yongdi, District Chief of the Sixth District, respectfully bow.

Second Installment 91

Report on the Implementation of Resolutions from the National Financial Conference

丨Compiled by the Committee for the Rectification of Local Taxes and Levies, Ministry of Finance丨

One. Introduction

The resolutions passed at this financial conference have been summarized in the first implementation report, detailing the Ministry of Finance's handling process. All major cases are expected to be organized and initiated before July 1st. Subsequently, the responsibility for promoting and maximizing benefits largely falls on the provincial and municipal governments for actual implementation. Since January, documents and reports from various parties concerning the abolition of excessive taxes and levies have been received. The progress made, sufficient to be announced to the nation, is categorized by province for reference. Additionally, seven points requiring attention are listed as follows:

1. The implementation of each case inevitably involves certain procedures. Provinces and cities face different situations, making immediate success impossible. The provincial reports announced in this issue represent the initial responses after the financial conference's conclusion. In the future, progress is expected to gradually extend outwards and advance systematically, meeting the nation's expectations.

2. The abolition of excessive levies cannot be separated from the rectification of local finances. Thorough planning and gradual advancement are essential for complete effectiveness. The reports in this issue only signify a fresh start for the people. Complete rectification is necessary to eliminate the long-standing financial malpractices of local areas and eradicate the root of excessive levies.

3. Among the resolutions, the rectification of land tax and the implementation of land registration are crucial. Many provinces are currently convening meetings to establish detailed implementation rules. Once the formal reports are submitted to the Ministry, they will be published successively.

4. Establishing local budgets is the foundation of financial rectification. Many provinces are separately convening county magistrates for small group meetings to ensure more thorough discussions on local budgets. Provinces like Jiangsu and Zhejiang have already submitted informal reports. Further details will be made public upon the conclusion of the process.

5. The central government's subsidies for local tobacco, alcohol, and license taxes have been allocated to local areas since July 1st. With direct management by local governments and leveraging local administrative power, tax revenues have increased. This greatly benefits the subsidy aspect. Allocation methods for stamp tax subsidies have also been determined, contingent on the extent to which each province abolishes excessive levies, followed by verification and allocation.

6. The central government attaches great importance to provincial and municipal donation and tax supervision committees. The selection of personnel must be meticulous. After extensive consultation, preliminary lists have been drafted. Starting next month, local supervision committees will be established successively.

7. On-site inspections are crucial for understanding local financial emergencies. Minister Kong of this Ministry has personally inspected the provinces of Hebei, Shanxi, Shandong, Shaanxi, Henan, and the cities of Beijing and Tianjin. Commissioners have also been dispatched to inspect the provinces of Chahar, Suiyuan, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Gansu, Ningxia, etc. Other provinces are continuously selecting and dispatching inspectors.

Time flies, and two months have passed since the financial conference's conclusion. One month remains until the July 1st deadline for abolishing excessive levies. During this period, responsible personnel have diligently striven, daring not to slacken. However, considering the nation's high expectations, the current reports may not fully satisfy them. Nevertheless, the rectification of local finances is extensive and complex. Ministry of Finance personnel dare not shy away from difficulties due to the arduous nature of the task, nor dare they be negligent due to the responsibility lying with local areas. Local financial authorities in each province and city are all striving to implement the conference's resolutions, making genuine progress. It is deeply believed that future facts will continue to prove this, satisfying the nation.

Two. Summary of Provincial Reports

The enthusiastic response of provinces and cities in implementing the financial conference's resolutions to abolish excessive taxes and levies, as seen in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hubei, Jiangxi, Hebei, Suiyuan, etc., is detailed in the first implementation report. More recently, provinces such as Shandong, Fujian, Hebei, Henan, Hunan, Anhui, Ningxia, Gansu, Chahar, etc., have been implementing phased abolitions of excessive levies since July 1st. Jiangsu is also continuing to abolish the second batch of 98 types of miscellaneous county levies. The details are as follows:

(1) Shandong Province: On July 14th, the Ministry approved the Shandong Provincial Government's report stating that the province's measures to abolish excessive levies in accordance with the financial conference's resolutions involve first abolishing provincial taxes that hinder central government revenue, such as tobacco leaf, trade, and yellow wine levies; those involving double taxation, such as meat market and theater levies; and those hindering transportation, such as road carriage, vehicle, foot, boat, and boat ticket levies, totaling 109,728 yuan (see Appendix 1). Together with various local county excessive levies totaling 31,174 yuan (see Appendix 2), the total amount abolished in the first phase is 141,562 yuan, which has been approved by the provincial government and implemented in July. The Ministry also approved the provincial government's reply stating that the Ministry's promulgated measures for rectifying business tax and merchant tax, reforming the land tax collection system, and eliminating temporary apportionments have been forwarded for compliance.

(2) Fujian Province: On July 17th, the Ministry approved the Fujian Provincial Government's report stating that Fujian Province, having suffered greatly from military conflicts, with the people deeply troubled by excessive levies, the Fujian Provincial Finance Department has abolished the most excessive and detailed taxes and levies in counties affiliated with the province, such as jasmine, chicken, goose, and duck levies, totaling 27 items with an annual amount of over 210,000 yuan (see Appendix 3). Investigations into the abolition of others are also underway. The Ministry also approved the provincial government's reply stating that the Ministry's promulgated measures for rectifying business tax have been submitted to the Finance Department for compliance. The Finance Department's report requesting a strict prohibition of arbitrary tax and levy increases beyond the regular tax has also been ordered to be followed. On July 25th, the Finance Department also reported that county regiment expenses had been proposed to the provincial government for abolition. If feasible, it is estimated that the province can reduce the people's burden by 900,000 yuan annually.

(3) Hebei Province: On July 10th, the Ministry approved the Hebei Provincial Government's report stating that Hebei Province has formulated implementation steps for abolishing excessive taxes and levies: (1) Abolishing provincial corvée, totaling 191,003 yuan annually; miscellaneous levies, totaling 60,010 yuan annually; and miscellaneous income, totaling 31,045 yuan annually, totaling 282,068 yuan. Also abolishing 90 types of county miscellaneous levies such as livestock transit levies, totaling 273,302 yuan annually (see Appendix 4), totaling 555,370 yuan. From July 1st, all those collected directly will be abolished. Those contracted to merchants with fixed terms ending before the end of December 1934 will be abolished upon expiration. Those with terms ending in 1935 should properly draft an advance abolition deadline, no later than the end of 1934, to comply with the general plan. (2) Supervising and ordering counties to properly draft abolition measures for the remaining levies, ensuring practical progress regardless of difficulties to achieve thorough implementation. (3) For the 51 counties where land tax surcharges exceed the regular tax, they have been reduced to within the regular tax range in accordance with the promulgated measures, and those equal to the regular tax, including Cang County and 31 other counties, have reduced a total of 799,000 yuan. The remaining 19 counties, including Wen'an, still need to reduce 596,000 yuan, and strict orders are still being given to reduce them within the deadline. The above has been submitted to the provincial government for approval and reported to the Ministry of Finance for record. The Ministry also approved the provincial government's reply stating that the Ministry's promulgated measures for rectifying business tax have been distributed to subordinates for prompt compliance and resubmission after review.

(4) Henan Province: On July 18th, the Ministry received a report from the Henan Provincial Finance Department stating that Henan Province's first batch of abolished excessive taxes and levies includes 14 types (see Appendix 5) and 37 types of land tax surcharges (see Appendix 6). The Finance Department also reported the following proposed abolition steps: (A) All miscellaneous levies existing in each county, whose nature, according to the interpretation agreed upon at the financial conference, can be regarded as illegal or excessively harsh, totaling 32 types with 264,572 yuan, will be abolished uniformly by the end of 1934 by general order to each county. (B) County deed tax surcharges exceeding half of the regular tax, totaling 234,915 yuan, will be abolished uniformly starting in 1935. (C) All types of voluntary donations and taxes and levies not belonging to the previous two categories, totaling 352,019 yuan, are planned to be gradually cleaned up and abolished. The Ministry also approved the provincial government's reply stating that the measures to reform the land tax collection system and eliminate temporary apportionments have been forwarded for compliance.

(5) Hunan Province: On June 28th, the Ministry received a letter from the Hunan Provincial Finance Department stating that among the miscellaneous levies in Hunan Province that are the most burdensome and cannot be completely abolished immediately, the only two are militia defense and education funds. Regarding the militia defense funds, the Security Command has already vigorously reduced and reorganized the militia teams throughout the province and unified the collection and distribution of all militia defense expenses. All types of miscellaneous levies collected by counties for militia defense funds in the past, totaling more than 50 types with an annual revenue of 1.6 million yuan (see Appendix 7), have been abolished uniformly. An order has been issued by the provincial government to implement the abolition from July 1st and to announce a ban, prohibiting them from being used for other purposes. As for the various miscellaneous levies collected for education and other purposes, efforts are currently being made to plan, understand the actual situation in each county, and gradually abolish them within a feasible range. Legal taxes and levies that should be rectified will also be thoroughly enforced. The letter also reported that the resolution from the financial conference prohibiting arbitrary additions to taxes outside the regular tax has been universally ordered for compliance. The provincial government's reply regarding the elimination of temporary apportionments has also been forwarded for compliance. (To be continued)

President Wang and his entourage arrived at their residence on Bubbling Well Road yesterday morning at 7:00 AM after taking the overnight train from Beijing.
