Cooperation is necessary to eliminate the communists, and separation of military and civilian affairs is necessary to govern. In addition to the talks, it turned out that what he called separation of military and civilian affairs only wanted to give me the position of Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, and important issues such as the spirit of cooperation, security plans, and communist suppression strategies were not mentioned at all. I saw his inconsistency and immediately declined tactfully. After he returns to the province, how he reports to the central government and neighboring provinces is still unknown, or he may even use this to publicize and confuse the public. It is difficult to predict. I believe that the political disorder and the people's suffering in Guizhou have reached their peak. Tracing the origin of the disaster, is it not all due to the negligence of those in power, the use of petty people, and the neglect of government affairs, the greed for pleasure, and the disregard for the people's livelihood? If we can thoroughly realize this, be open and honest, and work together to govern, we may be able to cooperate and achieve something. It is a pity that he does not pay attention to reality and hopes to perfunctorily meet. There is no determination to improve, nor is there a concrete plan. This is like climbing a tree to catch a fish. I have not seen its possibility. Guocai respectfully salutes," etc.

Submission from the Bankers Association

Requesting a Temporary Suspension of the Savings Bank Law

The Shanghai Bankers Association submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance yesterday regarding the amendment of the Savings Bank Law, which read: "Submitted for the matter of request. Recently, the member banks of the Association reported that they had received instructions from the Ministry on July 28 regarding the promulgation and implementation of the Savings Bank Law. According to the provisions of Article 9 of the law, each of the banks concurrently operating savings banks should submit government bonds and treasury bills equivalent to one-quarter of the total savings deposit balance, calculated at the market price, to the Central Bank immediately, obtain receipts, and submit them to the Ministry for verification. A letter has also been sent to the Central Bank to properly determine the custody measures, etc. How should this be handled? Please make a public decision. At the meeting held by the Association today (31st), it was unanimously agreed that government laws and regulations should be followed. However, since the promulgation of the Savings Bank Law, the Association, in view of the articles contained therein, has felt that many of them are difficult to implement in practice and have submitted a request to the Ministry for review and approval, and publicly recommended representatives to meet with Director Xu of the Ministry to explain the various difficulties. We are extremely grateful for his willingness to listen and promised to find a way to remedy them. The entire Savings Bank Law is still in the process of being submitted for amendment, and the submission of government bonds and treasury bills does not fully comply with the full text of Article 9 of the law. The banks of the Association have not yet been informed of the Central Bank's custody measures. It was resolved that, in order to protect depositors and to be serious about operations, Article 9 of the law should be temporarily suspended pending a decision on the entire Savings Bank Law. In addition to submitting the difficulties in implementing the law to the Executive and Legislative Yuan for selection, we should prepare a document and submit it to the Ministry for review and approval, and request instructions to comply. This is in the public interest. We respectfully submit."

Delegates to the National Labor Conference

Li Pingheng and Others Returned to China Yesterday 98

Excellent Results in the Election of Directors and Factory Inspections

Li Will Go to Beijing Tonight to Report and Return to Shanghai to Take Office

According to the Central News Agency, Li Pingheng and his party of seven, representatives of China to the 18th International Labor Conference, returned to Shanghai on the Italian postal ship Conte Verde at 11:00 AM yesterday. Li is scheduled to take the night express train to Beijing tonight to report on the progress of his participation in the conference. The details of his arrival in Shanghai are as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

The representatives to the International Labor Conference who arrived in Shanghai yesterday included Li Pingheng, First Government Representative; Bao Guohua, Advisor; and He Jing, Secretary; An Futing, Labor Representative; Cheng Haifeng, Advisor; Zhang Yi, Secretary; and Wang Zhisheng, Capital Representative. Qian Chengxu, Capital Advisor, remained in Europe due to other matters and will return to China in October. When the representatives arrived at the Jianghai Customs Pier at 11:00 AM, various organizations in Shanghai, including the China Industrial General Federation, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the National Federation of Commerce, the Machine Industry Association, and the General Labor Union, sent representatives to the pier to welcome them. After disembarking, they went to the China Hotel to rest. The China Industrial General Federation and the National Federation of Commerce held a public banquet at the Yiyou Society on Third Road at 6:00 PM last night and invited the representatives to report on the details of their trip to the conference. (The content of the report was roughly the same as the written statement released, and the length of the statement is omitted.)

Written Statement

After arriving in Shanghai, Government Representative Li Pingheng released a written statement saying that the results of attending the conference were very good. In addition to participating in the discussion of the agenda set by the conference, the mission entrusted to him when he left the country was (1) to participate in the election of the Board of Directors of the International Labor Organization, and (2) to negotiate the Shanghai Concession Factory Inspection Case. Both of these matters have achieved good results.

Elected as Director

China has never been successful in the election of directors. This time, with 60 votes out of 61, an absolute majority, China was elected as the second non-permanent director. Other elected countries include Spain, Poland, Finland, Argentina, Czechoslovakia, Brazil, and Mexico.

Factory Inspection

As for the Shanghai Concession Factory Inspection Case, it has been one of the main disputes between China and the Shanghai Concession in recent years. Negotiations have been ongoing for several years without results. At this conference, Representative Li raised this matter and received the support of representatives from various countries. Mr. Batter Liu, Director of the International Labor Bureau, replied that he would do his best to resolve this case in the short term after the meeting so that China's factory inspection could proceed smoothly. After the meeting, Representative Li also personally visited the United Kingdom and France and discussed solutions with French Minister of Labor Magoti, British Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs Stanhope, and Undersecretary of Labor Roman. The results were very satisfactory. This matter should be resolved satisfactorily in the short term.

Resolutions

The conference lasted for three weeks. In addition to the election of directors, the conference passed draft conventions on shift breaks in glass factories and relief for unemployed workers, and revised draft conventions on prohibiting night work for women and compensating for occupational diseases. In addition, several resolutions were passed. However, there were no concrete results on the reduction of working hours (from 48 hours per week to 40 hours), which was of concern to all parties, and it was reserved for discussion at the next conference.

Labor Organization

The reporter asked Representative Li about the situation of the International Labor Organization, as the Chinese people are not clear about the situation of the International Labor Organization. According to Representative Li, the International Labor Organization is a product of the 1918 Paris Peace Conference. At that time, representatives of various countries at the meeting believed that world peace, in addition to political issues, should also pay attention to economic and social issues. Therefore, special chapters were set up in the Treaty of Versailles and other treaties to establish the International Labor Organization to jointly seek solutions to global labor problems through international cooperation. A conference is held once a year, and each member state sends one labor representative, one capital representative, and two government representatives to organize it, which is the highest authority of the labor organization. The daily affairs of the organization are handled by the International Labor Bureau. The scale is quite large, with more than 500 staff members. Branches are set up in major countries. The Board of Directors of the International Labor Organization is the supervisory body of the Labor Bureau, and its status is equal to the Council of the International Labor Organization. There are 32 directors in total, with labor and capital each occupying eight seats, and government representatives occupying 16 seats. Among these 16 seats, eight seats are permanently held by the main industrial countries: the United Kingdom, France, Germany, Italy, Canada, Japan, India, and Belgium. The other eight seats are elected by the conference every three years. Although China is an original member of the Labor Organization, it has never been elected in the past 16 years. This is the first time it has been elected. There are currently 57 members of the Labor Organization, which is more than the members of the League of Nations.

Entering Beijing Tonight

Government Representative Li Pingheng is scheduled to take the night express train to Beijing tonight to meet with Minister Chen, report on the progress of the trip, and ask for instructions on the date of taking office as a director of the International Labor Conference, and then return to Shanghai to set off. Therefore, it is expected that he will not be able to attend the meeting of the Board of Directors of the International Labor Conference in October in time. As for the other representatives, they plan to compile a report in Shanghai before going to Beijing.

Circular from the Ministry of Finance

Method for Transporting Silver 99

Transport from Shanghai, Hankou, and Tianjin to the Interior

Requires a Passport Issued by the Ministry of Finance

The Ministry of Finance issued a directive yesterday to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Banking and Money Trade Association stating: "Concerning the matter that transporting silver requires application to the Ministry for a passport before transport can commence, the original purpose was to prevent the private minting of silver in the interior. All silver existing in the interior, except for that requested to be minted or exchanged for silver standard currency, is not allowed to be used. Now, to facilitate merchants and civilians, a further notice is hereby issued: henceforth, anyone transporting silver from the interior to Shanghai, Hankou, or Tianjin should follow established procedures at each customs station. However, anyone transporting silver from Shanghai, Hankou, or Tianjin to the interior, or transporting it between these three places, must, in accordance with the previous order, apply to the Ministry for a passport before transport can commence. Apart from informing the Jianghai, Jianghan, and Jinhai customs superintendents and the Inspector General of Customs for implementation, this order is hereby issued for compliance. This order."

Relief for the Drought in Gaoqiao 100

The Dredging Bureau Orders Workers to Continue Pumping Water for Over Sixty Hours

The Dagong News Agency reports that the severe drought in the Gaoqiao district of Pudong has been reported on several occasions. It is now known that the Social Affairs Bureau previously allocated a water pumping machine, which was installed in the Jiangjiazhai area of Donghai. Director Song Ziliang also expressed great concern about the agricultural disaster and agreed to instruct the relevant staff to continue pumping water for sixty hours. This severe drought in the district can thus be mitigated to some extent.

Hongkou Epidemic Hospital

Report on Consultations for July 104

Epidemic Atmosphere Intensifies Again in Eastern Shanghai

The Hongkou Epidemic Hospital on Tangshan Road, organized by the Ji Yi Charity Association, has been in operation for three years. It has been managed by Dou Yaoting, Zhu Shien, Ying Zuoqing, and Li Quancai. This year, Feng Bingnan joined as honorary president and Zhu Meixian as vice president, jointly responsible for the hospital. Therefore, the hospital's operations are thriving. The hospital's affairs are managed by Bao Kangning and Xu Zaigao as directors, divided into departments such as documentation, accounting, and general affairs. Although the organization has only six people, they can adequately handle various affairs. In terms of medical affairs, the directors are Zhu Xiaofang and Lin Chunshan, who have accumulated more than twenty years of experience in epidemic treatment and have gained many insights. They also have the support of renowned doctors such as Baodel, Fansier, and Bianlisi, and the responsible treatment of doctors Lin Xiongfei, Shi Yongqi, Zhang Zidao, and Jiang Hansheng. There are also four doctors interned in the hospital to gain experience. The pharmacists and nurses are also outstanding talents of the time. Therefore, those seeking treatment from far and near are like water flowing into a ravine, earning the trust of the public. Now, upon learning of the hospital's July report, it is promptly recorded below, which those concerned about the social situation will be pleased to hear. There were 12,692 outpatient visits, with 11,048 from the concession and 1,644 from the Chinese area, 818 return visits, 2,780 vaccinations, and a total of 1,606 hospitalizations, averaging 50 per day. There were 19 surgeries, more than 300 critical cases, and 8 patients who could not be saved. The hospital received $410 in first and second class hospitalization fees and $7,364.88 in donations from various sectors. The hospital's expenses have always been borne by the hospital directors, but because of its outstanding performance, donations from various sectors have been very enthusiastic. It is reported that recently, there have been 400 to 500 outpatient visits per day, mostly severe cases of dysentery, with temperatures above 104 degrees, requiring acupuncture treatment. The expenses are quite high. There are also several critical cases of heatstroke every day. Therefore, the epidemic situation is still increasing. The weather has been continuously sultry, the poor lack of hygiene, and there have even been cases of true cholera. Social concerns cannot be ignored.

Daxing Company

The Fuxing Vessel, Grounded, Safely Arrives in Shanghai 105

The Daxing Shipping Company's Fuxing vessel, operating the Shanghai-Chongsha route, ran aground on the evening of the 1st of this month. The vessel departed from Qidong for Shanghai, carrying a significant amount of passengers and cargo. That evening, while navigating near Miaogang in Chongming, due to a momentary oversight, it ran aground on a shallow sandbar. It was unable to get out of danger that night. The next day, vigorous attempts were made, but due to the heavy load and deep draft, they did not achieve their goal. The passengers on board, suffering from the heat and stuffiness, voluntarily waded to the shallow shore of Miaogang and then transferred to the Baohua vessel of the Ping'an Shipping Company to Shanghai. The poor passengers and merchants in steerage class, unable to afford another ticket, had to remain stranded until the evening of the second day. When the tide rose, the vessel broke free from the shallow beach at full speed, allowing it to escape danger and return to Shanghai. Although the cargo on board was not severely damaged in this grounding, a significant number of chickens, ducks, and fresh goods were lost due to the heat, starvation, death, and spoilage over the two days. After the Fuxing vessel arrived in Shanghai, it was inspected and found not to have suffered any damage to the hull, which is fortunate.

Page 12

Public Concession

The Rickshaw Problem Remains Serious 106

The Vehicle Committee Will Begin Distributing Business Licenses on the 7th

Public Discussion on the 6th; Rickshaw Owners Have Prepared Opinions

The Xinxin News Agency reports that the Shanghai Municipal Council convened both parties to discuss a solution to the rickshaw problem in the Public Concession, but due to the insistence of both parties, no result was achieved. Therefore, the severity of this problem remains far from optimistic. The following is a detailed account of the information obtained by the Xinxin News Agency reporter:

Rickshaw Association Statement

Yesterday, a responsible person from the Rickshaw Management Committee stated that although the chairman of the Council, Mr. Massey, also participated in the meeting convened by the Municipal Council to discuss with the rickshaw owners, this was only a preliminary discussion to gather opinions and did not involve any specific suggestions. The report that Mr. Massey firmly rejected the opinions of the rickshaw owners is not factual. As an affiliate of the Municipal Council, the Council has no authority to change its principles. The current opposition of rickshaw owners to the registration of rickshaw pullers is a misunderstanding. Labor relief in various countries is by no means based on a small amount of charity but must thoroughly improve the treatment of workers and provide their occupation with a corresponding guarantee, enabling them to maintain their minimum living standards. Otherwise, with too many monks and not enough gruel, everyone will be driven to desperation, which is not a reasonable method of relief. Rickshaw owners have stated that the death or illness of some of the 50,000 rickshaw pullers will affect business. This is not difficult to address, and the Council has its own methods to deal with it. As for raising fares, this is only a "hypothetical" standard price set by the Council. The Council will never force rickshaw pullers to comply and increase the burden on citizens. In short, the Council has never disregarded the difficulties of rickshaw owners. Looking at the Municipal Council's announcement of accepting the petitions of new rickshaw owners, a total of 4,893 new rickshaw owners have submitted petitions, requesting 47,580 public rickshaw licenses, all willing to comply with the new regulations. If the Council's new regulations cannot be implemented, how can these new rickshaw owners come to make this request? The Council has not yet determined the distribution of licenses but has prepared for it. Some applicants still need to be investigated, and once they have submitted their responses, the Vehicle Committee will proceed with the distribution. The licenses for August will be issued from the 7th to the 13th.

Public Association Opinion

After the Municipal Council held a meeting the day before yesterday, Director Zhong Sizeng instructed the representatives of the Rickshaw Trade Association to prepare minimum amendments to the new regulations to be presented for public discussion at the meeting at 10 AM on the 6th. It is now known that the Association has drafted seven items: (1) rickshaw rental issues; (2) rickshaw puller relief fund; (3) discussion of new rickshaw styles; (4) business protection (Items 1, 2, and 3 of the new regulations provide no protection for rickshaw owners' businesses); (5) rickshaw puller registration procedures; (6) deadline for rickshaw owners to obtain new licenses; (7) establishment of a rickshaw industry committee to assist in the implementation of the new regulations, etc.

Chinese Committee Conversation

The Guowen News Agency reports that the Shanghai Municipal Council, in order to improve the treatment and living conditions of rickshaw pullers in the special district, has specially drafted sixteen articles of a plan and is determined to implement them from August 1st. The rickshaw owners, however, believe that the content of the new regulations is too harsh and are also insisting on opposing them, so the August licenses cannot be obtained. According to custom, the license period for each quarter can only be extended by six days at the latest. After the deadline, continued business will not be allowed. Now, with only two days until the deadline, the rickshaw owners are quite anxious. It is likely that all rickshaws in the Public Concession will be suspended as a result, leading to a strike. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and other groups are also paying close attention to this and discussing solutions to avoid a breakdown between the two parties. The Guowen News Agency reporter specially inquired about this matter with Mr. Wang of the Vehicle Affairs Committee, who provided a detailed explanation, which is recorded below. According to him, the Municipal Council began to improve the treatment and living conditions of rickshaw pullers last year and established the Vehicle Affairs Committee to conduct a thorough investigation of the situation of rickshaw pullers and the layers of exploitation by rickshaw owners. The draft plan was also announced in February of this year and has been in effect for half a year. It is quite difficult to modify the content of the new regulations, as the Municipal Council has long been determined on this issue and there is no room for further modification. As for the current shady practices of rickshaw pullers renting rickshaws from rickshaw owners, they are obvious to everyone, and public opinion is clear. It is said that the Municipal Council once convened rickshaw owners to modify the new regulations, which would be inconsistent and contradict the facts. Although there was a public discussion, there were no resolutions, and this committee did not receive any formal orders. The new regulations implemented by the Municipal Council are based on the committee's investigation report. Even if there are slight changes, the consent of this committee must be obtained first. The rickshaw owners have raised many arguments recently, which are unfounded and difficult to establish. Those who are knowledgeable will understand. As for the advance payment of one yuan and five jiao, the Municipal Council has not determined its use or prepared a budget. The purpose of the Municipal Council in collecting this fee is to force rickshaw owners to seek happiness for rickshaw pullers. All funds are directly withdrawn by the rickshaw owners. The intention of the Municipal Council is only to be in a supervisory position. Some people say that the Municipal Council seems to be too arbitrary and hasty. In fact, this is not the case. The content of the report was announced in February of this year, which is now half a year ago. How can it be said to be too hasty? However, we sincerely welcome all sectors to investigate the content of both parties in detail and make a fair judgment. If the measures of the Municipal Council are indeed flawed, they can be criticized, deliberated, and modified. If everyone believes that there are no mistakes, we will not be intimidated by any threats, even if a strike occurs. As for the Fa Hua licenses, they have already been obtained. This matter is not related to the Municipal Council and cannot be interfered with. If the old rickshaw owners insist on maintaining their views, the Municipal Council has also decided to issue licenses to those who are willing to accept the new regulations. According to statistics, the new rickshaw owners who have submitted petitions currently number 4,893. Although the distribution of licenses has not been determined, preparations have been made for the distribution. If this incident remains deadlocked, from August 7th, all certificates and licenses will be issued to the new rickshaw owners who have applied to take over the business.

The Vehicle Affairs Committee was in a meeting at the time, so they appointed an officer named Yuan to receive them. As for the various plans that the Municipal Council is now implementing to relieve rickshaw pullers, the rickshaw pullers are deeply grateful. However, of the sixteen articles discussed, the board of directors has resolved to retain the first three articles, and only thirteen articles are currently being implemented. All those posing as rickshaw puller representatives, such as Feng Guisheng, are actually He Wushan, who used to be a stallholder, also known as Songqing, using the alias Jia Rui. He is a speculator who falsely poses as a representative group, admitting everything, using the Municipal Council, and spreading rumors abroad, disregarding the livelihood of rickshaw pullers. It is clear that he is a reactionary element who intends to disrupt. Today, Guoliang and others, entrusted by rickshaw pullers throughout the city, are requesting the following points from your office: (1) The rickshaw owners have now agreed to reduce the rickshaw rental to twelve jiao and donate one yuan per vehicle per month for rickshaw puller relief. The rickshaw pullers are satisfied with this and ask for a peaceful resolution to end the disputes and secure their livelihoods. (2) Please crack down on the police's random confiscation of licenses. Jointly Purchase 160,000 Shi of Foreign Rice 107

The cost, including tariffs, etc., is ten and a half yuan per 200 pounds

The Dagong News Agency reports that since the summer of this year, the weather has been arid and the price of rice has soared. The local rice industry once planned to purchase 500,000 shi of foreign rice to prepare for famine and to help suppress rice prices. However, after being unanimously opposed by various regions, a general meeting was convened to reconsider and cancel the plan. However, the atmosphere of ordering foreign rice has remained pervasive. According to a message from the rice industry yesterday, four local silver firms and six rice firms with strong capital from both the north and south markets have jointly purchased 160,000 shi of Saigon rice, which will be undertaken by the two British firms, Jardine Matheson and Daofu. The contract was signed the day before yesterday (the 3rd). Including import tariffs and transportation costs, the total cost is ten yuan and five jiao per 200 pounds, and each shi is 100 jin, which is equivalent to seven yuan and seven or eight jiao. The foreign rice will be ordered by the undertaking foreign firm to be shipped from the production area and is expected to arrive in Shanghai in early September, ready to be sold when the market price rises.

Landlord Company Orders Contract Signing

Residents of Xicheng Lane Petition for Relief 120

There are a total of 134 houses in Xicheng Lane on Ximen Road and Malang Road in this city, housing more than 2,000 residents. It is the property of Sun Chuanfang, the former Commander-in-Chief of the Five-Province Allied Forces, and was managed by the Yi Pin Bank. A rental contract was in place, and the relationship between the landlord and tenants was harmonious. This year, Yi Yuan Company took over the management. Unexpectedly, within three months, the company ordered the tenants to sign a new contract. Because the content was harsh, it was not accepted. Unexpectedly, the company, regardless of the situation, hired a lawyer to sue in the Second Special District Court, issuing an order for immediate eviction. The lane submitted petitions to the Municipal Social Bureau and the Second Special District Local Court yesterday, requesting relief. The petition stated that the houses in Xicheng Lane on Sima Road and Malang Road were managed by the Yi Pin Bank. This year, the management was suddenly changed to the Yi Yuan Company. During the change, the Yi Yuan Company sent a letter to the tenants stating that the change in the name of Yi Yuan Company was only nominal and that nothing else had changed. Unexpectedly, within three months, the company ordered the tenants to sign a new contract. After reviewing the contents of the contract, the tenants found it too harsh and unacceptable and requested revisions. Unexpectedly, the company, regardless of the situation, hired lawyer Wu Zhenming to file a lawsuit in the Second Special District Court for refusal to sign the contract, involving as many as 36 households. The company claimed that if the tenants did not sign the new contract, they would be evicted so that the company could re-let the houses, increase the rent, and collect kickbacks. The residents, based on legal principles and human sentiment, made a clear defense to the court. The court ruled to dismiss the plaintiff's lawsuit, but Yi Yuan Company continued to be litigious and filed an appeal. The residents believe that they rent houses to live in peace and that the company is now using the remaining power of the warlords to exert pressure and entangle them in lawsuits, causing them to live in unease. Moreover, according to Article 425 of the Civil Code, the lessee has the right to transfer a contract. The company is disregarding legal principles and relying on its power to bring lawsuits, causing the tenants to suffer unwarranted losses and inexplicable pain, with no way to appeal. Furthermore, the rent in Xicheng Lane was already increased by 10% in 1919. Now, at a time when business is declining and all industries are bankrupt, the residents are struggling to make a living, and such a large rent is unbearable. Therefore, various industries in the city have already reduced rents. The residents have organized the Xicheng Lane Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation to unanimously request a rent reduction to ease their burden. The residents are not making excessive demands, only requesting a 10% reduction to restore the rent to the level before 1919, which can be said to be justified. Therefore, we are specially submitting this petition to request your bureau to make a fair correction, and we earnestly request that the details be telegraphed to Mr. Sun Chuanfang, requesting that he notify the management office to approve the reduction and request the court to withdraw the lawsuit to avoid disputes and protect the safety of the tenants. We would be extremely grateful. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau.

Record of the Trial of the Zhoujiaqiao Assassination Case 123

Further Hearing to Be Held After Witnesses Are Summoned

Jin Menggen, a local resident of Dajingeng, Zhoujiaqiao, in western Shanghai, was an inspector at a yarn factory and ran the Shunxingyuan teahouse in Zhoujiaqiao. He had one wife and two concubines. He first married Wang, but because she was infertile, he took Liu as a concubine, but she still did not have any children. Therefore, he took Bao as a second concubine, who bore him two sons, the elder five years old and the younger two years old. Jin and Wang Xingshan (also known as A'xin, the former head of the Zhoujiaqiao Security Corps, who served from 1913 to 1916) had a feud because they jointly opened the Yongle Society Tanhuang Theater. In the beginning, Wang Qian was the manager, but after a dispute, the management position was taken over by another shareholder, Gao Maodi. At 5:30 AM on June 11 of this year (the 30th day of the fourth lunar month), Jin carried a birdcage and walked out of his home, Shunxingyuan, in Zhoujiaqiao, to fly his bird. Unexpectedly, about forty storefronts away from his home, he was shot and killed by his enemy. The court sent officials to investigate and determine the cause of death, and the police arrested Wang Xingshan, who was suspected of being involved, and sent him to the local court. Prosecutor Zhang Zi opened the trial several times and prosecuted him for murder, requesting a public trial in the criminal court. Yesterday morning, Judge Shao Qinzhi specially opened the Third Court to try the case. The defendant, Wang Xingshan, hired three lawyers, Yang Zhihao, Wu Kaisheng, and Shun Hanli, to appear in court to defend him. The deceased's wife, Jin Wang, was ill and did not attend. The deceased's concubines, Jin Liu and Jin Bao, attended the court and hired lawyer Sha Xunyi to request a private prosecution. Witnesses Qian Er, Wang Bugao, Gao Tongsheng, and others were present. After the judge took the stand, he ordered Wang Xingshan, who was in custody, to be brought to the dock to testify. He was 52 years old, from Shanghai, and lived in Zhoujiaqiao. He said that he did not go out on the morning of June 11. The judge asked if he had a "lao touzi" (a euphemism for a mentor or spiritual guide). He replied that he did not, but he had only taken Lu as his "xiansheng" (teacher) six years ago. The judge asked if there was a difference between "xiansheng" and "lao touzi." He replied that he did not know. The judge asked how many sworn brothers he had. He replied that he did not have any. The judge asked why he wanted to "bai xiansheng" (become a student/disciple). He replied that he opened a bathhouse and was afraid that someone would come to cause trouble. The judge asked how many years he had been running the bathhouse. He replied that it had been about three years. The judge asked if he had ever been the manager of the Yongle Society Tanhuang Theater. He replied that he had not. Then, Jin Liu, Jin Bao, and others requested that justice be done for their husband. Finally, after each witness testified, the judge said that it was necessary to summon more witnesses and scheduled another hearing. The defendant was taken back into custody.

More Than Twenty Attendees Including Yuan Ying

The government should actively promote it. (2) The sponsors of the society should separately be responsible for fundraising, which is currently underway. As soon as replies are received, a donation list will be made and they will be asked to donate. (3) Venerable elders from various mountains and Buddhist associations in various provinces, cities, and districts should be asked to solicit donations. (4) After the inaugural meeting is held, a donation team will be organized to raise funds.

Page 13

Zhang Jinfeng Used Name to Run School

Fraudulent Land Acquisition Case Concluded on Appeal 130

Trial Held Yesterday at the Jiangsu High Court, Verdict to Be Announced on the 8th of This Month

Guomin News Agency reports that Zhang Jinfeng (also known as Ji Lan), a well-known wealthy man from Jiangwan, used his position as the Director of General Affairs of the All-China Athletic Federation in 1921 to falsely claim that he would establish a school and factory. He obtained approval from Feng Cheng, the magistrate of Baoshan County, to acquire more than 230 mu of civilian land at low prices in the "Yin Jiu" and "Yin Shi Yi" areas of Jiangwan. He then leased the land to the Japanese to be used as a volleyball field, but the school and factory were never established. It was also heard that he had sold the land to foreign merchants. The original landowners learned of this and submitted petitions to party and government agencies in 1927, requesting that he be brought to justice.

Taken into Custody and Sent to Court

At that time, the Shanghai Branch of the Central Political Council resolved to issue a warrant for his arrest and investigation, but Zhang was powerful and influential and remained at large. After the establishment of the municipal government, the case was handled by the municipal government. In October 1929, the municipal government announced that the land could not be bought or sold or mortgaged, and instructed the Land Bureau to announce the suspension of transfer registration. At the same time, Zhang was taken into custody and sent to court. Later, with the help of a certain important person, he was released on bail of 50,000 yuan, and the case was shelved for years until July 1930.

No Prosecution

After investigation, the Procuratorate of the Local Court decided not to prosecute. Subsequently, the municipal government, based on public opinion and facts, sent a letter to the court requesting reconsideration, but without result. In November of last year, the Local Court suddenly received an order from the Higher Court, forwarded from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, stating that the original decision was inappropriate and instructing that it be revoked. The court then conducted a re-investigation in accordance with legal procedures and decided to prosecute.

Surrendered and Taken into Custody

On the afternoon of April 16, Zhang himself, for some reason, went to the court with his lawyer and was taken into custody. On May 13, the court debate concluded and he was sentenced to five years in prison. The lawyer requested bail, but it was denied. Zhang was dissatisfied and appealed to the Higher Court.

Scheduled for Pronouncement

Yesterday was the date for the hearing of this case. The plaintiffs, the original landowners Zhong Dunyao, Hou Maomao, Shen Yueqing, and Li Baobao, as well as the defendant Zhang Jinfeng and lawyer Jiang Yiping and two others, were present. After the judges questioned them separately, the lawyers made their defense. The judges announced that the verdict would be announced on the 8th.

Giant Robbery Case Seven Years Ago

Accomplice Arrested 132

Comprador Suspected of Being an Inside Informant

At Large for a Long Time, Recently Arrested

The Beilaiheng Foreign Firm, owned by a Spaniard, located at No. 320 Jiangxi Road, specializes in the business of pearl jewelry and gold watches, with a wide range of operations. At midnight on May 21, 1927, the safe in the foreign firm where jewelry was stored was suddenly pried open, and all the jewelry and 1,352 gold watches, worth 50,000 yuan, were stolen. The next morning, the foreign firm discovered the theft and reported it to the General Patrol Station, requesting an investigation. After a detailed investigation by the patrol station, two suspects, a Russian named Si Deluonai and a Cantonese named Li Yuhua, were arrested. A portion of the stolen goods, gold watches worth 5,000 yuan, were found. Li claimed to be Portuguese and had been naturalized as a Portuguese citizen, so the patrol station sent Li to the Portuguese Consulate, which transferred him to the Macau Consulate, where he was sentenced to two and a half years in prison. The patrol station sent the Russian Si Deluo to the former Provisional Court, but before the case was concluded, the Russian committed suicide in the patrol station. However, Li's confession implicated the Chinese comprador of the foreign firm, a Cantonese named Chen Jiansheng, as an accomplice in the case. The patrol station also confirmed that Chen was indeed in a suspicious position. The foreign firm had four safes, large and small, and the key to the smaller safe was hidden in each safe, while the remaining safes contained jewelry. When the theft occurred that night, the thieves first managed to blow up the small safe to obtain the key, and then opened the large safes and took the important jewelry. The thieves were very familiar with the internal situation of the firm, so there must have been an inside informant. Therefore, the patrol station paid close attention to Chen Jiansheng and was about to arrest him.

Chinese Institute of Engineers

Building Materials Testing Laboratory 133

The location is in the city center; the cornerstone laying ceremony was held this morning.

The Chinese Institute of Engineers, in view of the fact that there is no dedicated testing facility for various materials in Chinese industry, which makes it impossible to assess the quality of products, and both production and sales are greatly affected, established the Architectural and Industrial Materials Testing Laboratory Committee in the spring of the 18th year. Shen Yi, Wang Boqiao, Xue Cixin, Xu Enzeng, and others were hired as members, and a base was purchased in Fenglin Bridge in the new western district of the city for future use. Subsequently, the board of directors of the committee decided to rebuild in the central urban area due to the remote location of Fenglin Bridge. Therefore, it also purchased four acres of land in the area from the municipal government as the site of the testing laboratory. The drawings of the laboratory building were designed by architect Dong Dayou. The entire building is divided into three parts: the middle two floors are for offices, and the east and west parts are for testing rooms, each with an area of sixty square meters. The structural form adopts the latest cubic style, decorated with Chinese ornaments. The walls are made of stone, and the overall appearance expresses simplicity and solidity. If it is not sufficient in the future, another floor can be added. The funds for this project were raised from various sources, and a large number of building materials were donated by domestic industrial circles, such as the Yanghui donated by Qixin Cement Company and Shanghai and China Cement Companies, tiles from Yizhong Machinery Company and Xingye Tile Company, famous stones from China Stone Company, facing bricks from Taishan Brick and Tile Company, wiring devices from Huatong and Huasheng Electric Appliance Factories, wood from fans and motor Jiu Ji Timber Company, steel windows from Dongfang and Shanghai Steel Window Companies, terrazzo from Huachang Firm, bricks from Dazhong Tile Company, gravel from Yongda Stone Rolling Factory, and lime from Jinfeng Mineral Ash Factory, etc. The initial building of the testing laboratory has been contracted by Zhang Yutai Architectural Firm for 32,500 yuan, and the cornerstone laying ceremony will be held at 9:30 this morning (5th). After its completion in the future, the scope of testing and research will temporarily focus on the four industrial materials of machinery, chemistry, electrical engineering, and physics. However, the cost is huge, and it is hoped that all sectors will actively contribute to its completion. Regarding the testing application machines, it is also heard that the Swiss Amsler Testing Machine Company has donated a 3,000 kg large impact testing machine free of charge. It is also hoped that various manufacturers will donate as much as possible, so as to create a great testing institution and make the greatest contribution to the national industry and commerce.

When the arrest was about to take place, Chen learned about it and fled without a trace. He then petitioned the court to issue a warrant for his arrest, which has been ongoing for seven years without success. It was not until 12 noon the day before yesterday that Chief Detective Che Xueceng of the General Patrol Room learned that Chen had come to Shanghai from Suzhou and was hiding in Yule Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei. He went to arrest him and met Chen by chance at the intersection of Laobazi Road and Jiangxi Road. He was arrested and taken to the patrol room for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special Court's Criminal Division 1, where the patrol room lawyer Gan Jingxian prosecuted the defendant Chen Jiansheng for theft in accordance with Article 338 of the Criminal Law. Chen Jiansheng was a comprador in the Belle Hingham Foreign Firm, but he had resigned two months before the theft occurred and went to work for Baosheng Foreign Firm. However, ten days before the incident, he went to Suzhou to recuperate due to illness. He denied colluding with the theft, saying that it was Li Yuhua's false accusation, because Li and I were fellow villagers. Before, he colluded with a Westerner to falsely sign my name in an attempt to fraudulently claim 14,400 yuan, resulting in a grudge, etc. After reviewing the confession, Judge Qian Hongye ordered the case to be adjourned for seven days for further questioning, and the defendant was allowed to be released on bail for 10,000 yuan.

Falsely Establishing a Company to Defraud Goods 134

Using Bounced Checks as a Cover

Fourteen Victims

| Suspects Arrested in Shanghai and Hangzhou |

Baoyuanshang Department Store, located at No. 2 Ruyili, Lan Weiai Road, French Concession, was opened on May 24 this year. Shareholder and manager Zhou Ruiqing obtained two shares, Qiu Zhenhua, manager of Huadong Department Store of Shanghai Military Camp, obtained one share, the owner of Gu Tianbao Silver Shop on Gordon Road obtained one share, Wang Xuelin from Tongzhou (formerly a detective in the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau) obtained one share, and Chen Ziming obtained one share, totaling seven shares. However, the shareholders did not contribute capital. It was actually a fictitious and slippery company that defrauded goods from various shops and factories in Shanghai. Chen Ziming established Yichangshun United Company in Hangzhou. Their method of defrauding goods in Shanghai was to have Gu Tianbao Silver Shop and Huadong Department Store issue bounced checks to various customers to defraud goods, which were transported to Hangzhou at night for sale and profit sharing. On the 17th of last month, because the issued checks were due, the customers could not collect the money. At the same time, Baoyuanshang went bankrupt, and Zhou and others fled without a trace. The next day, creditors Shenkang Firm, Guosheng Industrial Raw Materials Firm, Mingguang Company, Xiangfu Factory, Mingfeng Firm, Dehua Firm, Xie Xing Sports Equipment Firm, Rimingxin Firm, Detai Xin Firm, Daming Socks Factory, Minsheng Trading Company, and other fourteen companies discovered that the goods defrauded from each company were worth about 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. Therefore, Yu Boji, representative of Shenkang Firm, and others reported to the French patrol room. Detectives Zhou Bingcheng and others successively arrested Baoyuanshang shareholders Wang Xuelin, Chen Ziming, and clerk Gao Depei in Shanghai and Hangzhou. They were first sent to the First Special District Court for prosecution in the primary court and transferred to the local court for trial. Yesterday, Judge Li Changnian interrogated them in Criminal Division 1. The patrol room lawyer Yao Zhaodi changed the charge to fraud in accordance with Article 363 of the Criminal Law. Wang Xuelin and Chen Ziming admitted to establishing a fictitious company to defraud goods. Gao Depei confessed to being a street vendor and denied colluding with the fraud. The plaintiffs also hired lawyers to request incidental civil suits to recover the defrauded money. The defendants also hired lawyers to defend themselves. After reviewing the confession in court, the debate was declared over, and the judgment was scheduled for the 9th of this month. Wang and Chen were remanded in custody, and Gao Depei was allowed to be released on bail pending a decision.

Mother Accuses Son and Daughter-in-Law of Assault 135

Judge Advises Reconciliation

The Case Still Needs Investigation

Cheng Yuangao, a student at Zhengfeng College and a native of Anhui County, is 22 years old. His wife, Yu Dihua, is from Beijing and Anhui and lives with Cheng at No. 8 Guirenli, Maigen Road. Cheng's mother, Huang, suddenly complained to the Xinzha Patrol Room that her son and daughter-in-law had assaulted her at home at 10 pm on the 26th of last month and injured her, requesting detention and investigation. The head of the patrol dispatched detectives to send her to Guangren Hospital for examination, where it was found that only the index finger of her right hand was slightly broken. The patrol room then filed a public prosecution in the First Special Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhan Liangce opened the Criminal Division 2 to summon Cheng Yuangao and Yu Dihua, accompanied by defense lawyer Sun Zuji, to court. The patrol room lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated that, according to the plaintiff's complaint, on the 26th, the door was closed when she went out, preventing the defendant from entering, which led to the assault. The patrol room is now prosecuting in accordance with Articles 293, 1 and 2 of the Criminal Law, and presented the injury report to the court. Huang from Cheng continued to claim that Cheng Yuangao was adopted by me at the age of one, and I married him at the age of eighteen. Now that he has grown up, he hates me and beats me under the pretext, and should be punished according to the law. Questioning Cheng Yuangao, he confessed that he was not at home that day, but was talking with Zheng Qiao, the owner of Zheng Qiao Long Foreign Goods Store on Hengfeng Road, Zhabei, with a letter from Zheng as proof, so I really didn't know anything. Lawyer Sun immediately rose and said that the plaintiff in this case had been involved in a lawsuit with his clansman Cheng Shi for the inheritance for seven or eight years. The plaintiff won the final victory, and Zheng Shuming (i.e., Zheng Yangqiao's brother) has a special relationship with Cheng Huang. Food and accommodation are provided by him. Now the plaintiff listens to Zheng's slander and intends to subject the defendant to criminal punishment in order to enjoy the huge inheritance alone. Therefore, the inside story of this case is extremely tortuous. If the plaintiff does not withdraw the case, the defendant will declare everything to the court. Questioning Yu Dihua, she confessed that on the 26th of last month, when my mother-in-law was not at home, I went out shopping. Unexpectedly, Zheng Shuming closed the door, preventing me from entering. I argued with him because he had nothing to do with Cheng and was always bored at home. He had no right to stop me from entering. At that time, the plaintiff also participated, but there was no assault. The court believed that the two parties in this case were mother and son and should not confront each other in court. Therefore, it advised the plaintiff to consider carefully, be calm, and not want to go to extremes. On the one hand, it also warned the defendant as a junior, no matter what the facts are, he must please his parents. Now that he is involved in a lawsuit, he should apologize to the plaintiff so that the relationship can be restored. Moreover, this case still needs to be investigated, and ordered a new hearing and ordered the two parties to try to reconcile.

Zhang Aizhen Sentenced for Assaulting Maid 141

A Letter to the Ministry of Justice and Administration for Remedy

Lawyer Zhang Tianyin of the Public Works Bureau filed a public prosecution with the Second Special District Court. Subsequently, Zhang Aizhen admitted in court that she had beaten her. Judge Wu Tingqi questioned the victim according to Article 293 of the Criminal Law for minor injury, and the court ruled not to prosecute, and Xiaobao was handed over to Zhang Aizhen to take back. It was reported earlier in this newspaper that the association believes that the victim Xiaobao is only six years old, and whether she has the ability to express her wishes is still a question. Even if she does, it cannot be used as a basis for judgment. Moreover, where are Xiaobao's biological parents, it is impossible to find out. Even if they are found, they may give up their right to sue on her behalf due to emotions and difficulties. In order to thoroughly protect the happiness of children and maintain humanity, the ruling in this case seems to be inappropriate in terms of law and human sentiment. Therefore, it yesterday listed the facts and opinions and sent a letter to the Ministry of Justice and Administration to request a remedy so that the victimized child can enjoy legal benefits and seek a definite legal guarantee for general children.

The weather in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River is sunny and hot, gradually becoming cloudy, with winds from the southwest to west. In this area and the East China Sea, the wind is from the southeast to northeast. The centers of two typhoons in the Pacific Ocean are still slowly moving northwest or northwest-west. The center of the first typhoon was located within 120 miles of the intersection of 18 degrees north latitude and 128 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM, stalling. The wind force is unknown. The center of the second typhoon was located within 120 miles of the intersection of 19 degrees north latitude and 137 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM, moving northwest-west or northwest. The wind force is unknown. Furthermore, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 100.4, and the lowest was 75.4. Reading Q&A

What is an International Issue? 147

丨丨 Answer to Mr. Gu Qianli

(1) The World is Humanity's Stage

What is an international issue? Before answering this question, it is necessary to first address what our world is. International issues occur within this world and are the main performances on this "world" stage. Therefore, before discussing the play, it is necessary to explain the stage.

The world, as commonly referred to, is the Earth, with a diameter of approximately 3,240 miles and an area of approximately 33 million miles. Land accounts for 29.2% of it, and oceans account for 77%. It is the home of all living things and the grand stage for humanity.

On this sphere, except for Antarctica's 14 million square kilometers and the Arctic's 2 million square kilometers, there are probably humans everywhere. The total human population is now approximately 1.7 billion.

Who built this stage? It was the great Mr. Nature. It existed before humans arrived in the world. Its history is too long, and we will not delve into it for now. But when did humans arrive on this stage? It is a long story. We know that they have been putting on "decent" plays on this stage for six or seven thousand years. Before that, for about 500,000 to 1 million years, their footprints were indeed on this stage, playing a more advanced role than their cousins丨丨apes丨丨. However, these old accounts cannot be detailed in this book.

Human understanding of this stage has undoubtedly gone through a long process. Not to mention that the world recognized by humans six or seven thousand years ago is not the world of today, even the world recognized by Chinese people eighty or ninety years ago is not the world of today. In the past, the world stage was obstructed by the stage equipment of oceans, mountains, rivers, and deserts. Humans were limited by nature, living in small environments in groups, with little communication between groups. Therefore, they each recognized that small world as the world, not knowing that the world they recognized was just a fragment of the whole, and that there were other brothers living like them beyond. (To be continued)

Lin and Zheng Win Doubles in Straight Sets

(Special Dispatch from Tianjin, 4th) In the second doubles match of the Tianjin-Shanghai Inter-Port Tennis Tournament, Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia (Shanghai) defeated David and Kuwahara (Tianjin) in straight sets. The scores were 6-0 in the first set, 6-4 in the second, and 6-4 in the third. In the third singles match, Carlsen (Shanghai) defeated Xia Guanfu (Tianjin) 3-1. The scores were 6-4 in the first set, 3-6 in the second, 6-3 in the third, and 6-1 in the fourth. The first doubles match between Carlsen and Boninifer (Shanghai) and Xiao Longgan and Er Longgan (Tianjin) will be held at the British tennis court tomorrow afternoon.

Lin and Zheng Score a Great Victory in Doubles 150

Today's Tianjin-Shanghai tennis match was held on time at 3:00 PM at the British tennis court. The audience was still over a thousand people. First up was the second doubles match between Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia against Kuwahara and David. Lin and Zheng coordinated well, taking the advantage from the start. Baohua's backhand smashes and Zhaojia's interceptions each displayed their strengths, making it impossible for David and Kuwahara to retaliate. They won the first set 6-0. This set was won very easily. In the second set, Kuwahara and David tried their best to counterattack, but they were contained by Xiao Zheng's interceptions. The outcome of the third set was already decided. David's smashes went out of bounds, making Kuwahara helpless and negatively impacted. They both failed 6-4. Lin Baohua and Zheng Zhaojia (Shanghai) 6-0, 6-4, 6-4, Kuwahara and David (Tianjin).

Carlsen Defeats His Opponent with Ease 151

Next was the third singles match. Xia Guanfu entered the court with great momentum, competing with Carlsen for victory. In the second set, Xia took the advantage with effective swings. The third set was crucial for the outcome. Carlsen used a calm demeanor, and his tactics were enough to overcome the strong opponent. By the fourth set, the outcome was no longer in question. Carlsen played with even more ease, but Xia Guanfu was already exhausted, and thus failed in succession.

Educational News

Northeast Student Subsidies

14,000 Per Month 166

2,600 Quotas for General Subsidies

2,080 Quotas for Special Subsidies

The Ministry of Education's Northeast Youth Relief Office has finalized the measures for subsidizing students from the Northeast in the country. The office has determined two types of subsidies: general subsidies (i.e., food expenses) and special subsidies (i.e., books and daily necessities). The total monthly subsidy required for students at all levels of schools is 14,000 yuan. The subsidies will begin to be issued this semester. The number of quotas to be subsidized for each level of school and the distribution of the monthly subsidy per person are as follows: (1) For colleges and universities, there are 900 quotas for general subsidies, with a monthly allowance of 4 yuan per person; there are 480 quotas for special subsidies, with a monthly allowance of 5 yuan per person, totaling 6,000 yuan. (2) For high schools and equivalent schools, there are 900 quotas for general subsidies, with 3.5 yuan per person per month; there are 350 quotas for special subsidies, with 3 yuan per person per month, totaling 4,200 yuan. (3) For junior high schools and equivalent schools, there are 800 quotas for general subsidies, with 3.5 yuan per person per month; there are 250 quotas for special subsidies, with 2 yuan per person per month, totaling 3,300 yuan. (4) There are no general subsidies for primary schools for the time being, but there are 1,000 quotas for special subsidies, with 3 yuan per person per semester, totaling 500 yuan per month. The above statistics show that there are a total of 2,600 quotas for general subsidies and 2,080 quotas for special subsidies, totaling 14,000 yuan per month.

Municipal Education Bureau

Director Pan Speaks on Vocational Education 169

Broadcasted on the Greater China Radio Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau broadcasted on the Greater China Radio yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM. Director Pan spoke on vocational education. The original text is as follows:

Vocational education, through the promotion and efforts of various parties, seems to have a flourishing phenomenon at present. However, what exactly is vocational education? The general public is still unclear about it. If I still want to answer this question, I must first know what education is and what a vocation is. Education, I can still say, is the superstructure of society. It changes with changes in the social environment and economic conditions. Its task must be to meet the requirements of the times and complete the mission of the times, and to cultivate the younger generation to continue the affairs of the previous era. Therefore, the content, purpose, and form of education are different in each era. As for the word "vocation," according to the usage in the "Historical Records" cited in the "Ciyuan," a vocation is something that should be done within one's duty. According to the Webster's Dictionary, it can be translated as "any service rendered to society, whether directly or indirectly increasing productivity, is called a vocation."

Now that we have clarified the explanations of education and vocation, then what is vocational education? It is very easy to solve. We can say that vocational education is using educational methods to enable everyone to obtain appropriate vocations, so as to become sound members of society. Its purpose is to transform the unemployed and unemployed into employed, to consolidate and improve the status of the employed, and to increase productivity for the country and society. Currently, many people do not clearly analyze the factors for the success of vocational education and think that technical education is vocational education, but it is only teaching techniques related to various crafts. In fact, this is not the case. Skill is certainly one of the main elements of the success of vocational education, but in addition to this, there must be a very sufficient basic common sense. At the same time, in addition to general knowledge and specialized skills, there must also be a considerable character. The so-called technical education can only increase a little productive capacity, but it cannot guarantee the fulfillment of vocational life. If we can only produce but do not have the temperament, character, and moral concepts to coordinate and guide, then that person is equal to a machine. Therefore, technology is only a part of vocational education, and not the entire vocational education. This is a point that deserves special attention.

Since the explanation of vocational education is as described above, then its origin must also be briefly studied. The origin of vocational education, in a broad sense, can be said to have originated when humans had vocations. When there are vocations, people must be taught to continue and pass on from generation to generation. However, the source of the current so-called vocational education is as follows: (1) Artization of curriculum content. In the mid-seventeenth century, famous educators in Europe, such as Locke and Comenius, advocated that education should not focus on textbooks, but should focus on practice. Therefore, they advocated sensory training. When it came to Rousseau, he advocated that physical activity should not only strengthen the body, but also make the senses sensitive and the hands and brain work together. In "Emile," he advocated using the method of investigating industry and commerce to enable children to understand the actual situation of society, and children should practice woodworking in families and schools. When it came to Pestalozzi, he put it into practice, which can be regarded as the first experiment in the artization of curriculum content. Later, Fellenberg and Froebel continued, and it gradually became popular in the nineteenth century, especially in Northern European countries, such as the work training in Russia and the so-called technical system in Sweden, Denmark, Norway, and Finland. (2) Vocationization of school education. Because recent school graduates or dropouts have no skills to make a living when they go to society, there is a slogan that "graduation is unemployment." As a result, they have become high-level idlers. Therefore, educators have to find ways to remedy this, and they believe that the only remedy is to set up vocational courses in schools to make up for this deficiency.

The prevalence of vocationalization in Western schools is attributed to the Morrill Act in the United States. The motion of this act was because Professor Durrell proposed to allocate government land to various states as funding for establishing industrial schools. It was signed by Lincoln in 1862. Since then, vocational schools in the United States have flourished. Other countries, such as Japan, have followed the example of the United States, and China has followed the example of Japan. Recently, it has been learning from European and American countries, and everything is being actively implemented.

There are three main reasons why vocational education has gradually become consistent until recently, and it has a widespread trend in Europe and the United States. In China, although various parties have made efforts to promote it, it seems to have a flourishing atmosphere, but there are still many difficulties. (1) Outdated concepts, (2) difficulties for students in enrollment and employment, (3) social constraints, etc. If the above-mentioned difficulties cannot be resolved, then vocational education will be difficult to popularize.

Organized by the Municipal Education Bureau

Preliminary Exhibition of Labor Subject Achievement Products 170

Instructing Vocational Schools and Primary and Secondary Schools to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an instruction to municipal and registered private vocational schools and primary and secondary schools, stating that, in accordance with the Ministry of Education's order to hold the National Vocational School and Primary and Secondary School Labor Subject Achievement Product Exhibition of the 23rd year, the schools have been instructed to comply with it. Now, in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the above-mentioned exhibition methods, a preliminary exhibition of the city's labor subject achievement products will be held for selection and to select the best products to be sent to the Ministry. The schools' products should pay attention to the quality of the products, not just the quantity. The dates, venues, product scope, and procedures for sending products to the exhibition have been separately stipulated. In addition to distributing them separately, a copy of the measures is urgently attached below for your school to follow.

Measures for the Preliminary Exhibition of Labor Subject Achievement Products in Shanghai 171

(1) The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau will hold the city's preliminary exhibition of labor subject achievement products in accordance with Article 4 of the Ministry of Education's measures for holding the National Vocational School and Primary and Secondary School Labor Subject Achievement Product Exhibition of the 23rd year, and these measures will be formulated and implemented. (2) The conference will have one director of affairs, who will be responsible for all matters of the conference. There will be two departments: affairs and storage, each with one department director. The affairs department will be divided into three groups: communication, documentation, and general affairs. The storage department will be divided into three groups: layout, management, and registration. Each group will have one chief secretary and several secretaries. (3) The exhibition venue will be located in the Shangwen Primary School in Yongning Road, Xueqian Street, South Shanghai District. Office hours are from 8:30 AM to 5:00 PM daily. (4) The exhibition schedule is set for August 29, 30, and 31, lasting three days. The exhibition dates are from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM daily. (5) The scope of products and matters that should be paid attention to when exhibiting products should comply with the provisions of Articles 10 and 15 of the exhibition measures promulgated by the Ministry of Education. (6) All schools participating in the exhibition should submit two copies of the product list (according to the format issued by the Ministry) to the Municipal Education Bureau for registration before August 10 and collect labels for pasting on each product. (7) The schools' products should be sent to the exhibition for display starting at 8:30 AM three days before the opening of the conference (August 26). (8) The display of achievement products will be based on schools, indicating the product category. (5) When schools send and display products, the director of the storage department will, together with the staff of each group, inspect and receive them in accordance with the product list and registration form, and issue receipts. (10) After the products are inspected and received, the staff of the exhibiting school will distribute and display them on their own according to the designated display location. (11) During the exhibition period, visitors should be received by each group. If there are any questions, they should be explained by the representative or reception staff of the exhibiting school. (12) The evaluation of the exhibited products will be based on schools, and grades such as A, B, C, and D will be recorded. The standards for the evaluation method will be formulated separately. (13) Except for the achievement products that represent the achievement products and are retained for display by the Ministry of Education, the schools' exhibited products should be brought back to the conference with the original receipt within two days after the closing of the conference. The conference will not be responsible for safekeeping after the deadline. (14) These measures will be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Savings 191

— Thin Autumn

Saving is the act of accumulating money that has been saved. Because a person living in the world inevitably encounters disasters, illnesses, and all sorts of unexpected accidents. If one does not have savings during ordinary times, how can one cope with these unexpected accidents? Therefore, saving is indeed a virtue.

The methods of saving can be roughly divided into two types: one is saving in whole numbers, and the other is saving in small amounts. The former can only be done by people with ample financial resources, while the latter can be done by anyone. For example, there is a child whose father gives him ten cents of silver every day for snacks and candy. What does he do? He only spends twenty copper coins each day, saving the remaining ten coins. At the end of each month, he exchanges them for one silver dollar and deposits it in the bank. If he keeps doing this without interruption, he will have a savings of four hundred and seventeen yuan after fifteen years. Moreover, this savings only includes a principal of one hundred and eighty yuan, with the remaining two hundred and thirty-seven yuan being interest. This is the method of accumulating small amounts into a large sum, gathering a fur coat from fox scraps. If this child did not save ten copper coins every day, he would certainly not have this savings.

Children! Are you willing to save? Then please start saving from today. It would be better if you can save ten copper coins every day, but if not, five or three coins are also fine. As long as you persevere, you will naturally have a substantial sum of money.

The Fearless Marconi 192

— Quan Jia

Children, when you listen to the radio, you probably always think of Marconi's great achievements for us. But he did not succeed by luck. His family was very poor, but he still diligently studied radio. When he first completed his first radio machine, he was extremely proud. He borrowed money and wanted to go from Italy to England to visit a well-known radio expert.

At that time, it was during the war. The customs inspector checked his radio and mistakenly thought it was military equipment. Although Marconi tried hard to explain, no one believed him, and it was eventually thrown into the sea.

Marconi suffered this failure and was plagued by poverty and illness, but he did not lose heart. He continued his research and finally invented this useful thing, contributing it to the world.

Children, what do you think after hearing this story? Failure is not shameful. Being discouraged after failure is the most useless thing. Things in the world often succeed after failure!

Poor Ice Boy 193

— Yi Zhen

Ice Boy was pressed under the ice bucket, unable to breathe. So he slowly climbed upwards, wanting to climb out of the ice bucket to cool off a bit.

Ice Elder saw this and asked, "Where are you hurrying to?" Ice Boy replied:

"I want to go outside, I really can't stand the stuffiness inside!"

Hearing this, Ice Elder said in a panic, "You can't go! You can't go! It's very dangerous outside. There are tigers outside, the sun will swallow you, there are poisonous snakes, the wind will blow you away. Just sit inside peacefully!"

Ice Boy didn't listen, saying, "I'm not afraid of tigers and poisonous snakes outside. Look, they have never come in!"

"Child! That's right, but we are united inside. If we are united, they won't dare to invade or oppress us. But when you go outside, they will definitely bully you because you are alone."

Ice Boy wouldn't listen! He kept climbing upwards. Just as he stepped onto the top of the bucket, suddenly there was a "snap" and he fell, shattering into pieces, and was swallowed by the tigers and the sun.

Children! Remember: As a child, you must not be stubborn. You must be adaptable in everything you do. See, didn't Ice Boy lose his life because of stubbornness?

Bing Er was a lively and innocent child, usually jumping around happily. Last night, for some reason, he suddenly clutched his stomach and cried out in pain, his eyebrows furrowed, looking very distressed. Mother asked anxiously, "Weren't you eating lunch just fine this morning? How did you suddenly get a stomachache? Did you eat something?" Bing Er didn't dare to hide anything and told the truth, "After I finished lunch today, I was very thirsty, so I bought a cup of ice cream and three cents worth of watermelon at the entrance of the alley. Who knew that before long, I would feel a dull pain in my abdomen, and now it's getting worse and worse, it feels like something is tightly squeezing it!"

Later, Bing Er recovered from his illness and never dared to buy things randomly on the street again.
