I Know 195

— Su Su

Miss Cicada put on a light gauze dress and lived in a villa built of leaves. In the morning, she drank some sweet dew, at noon she sang a few songs, and in the evening, she lay on the well-ventilated branches to cool off. She thought that her destiny was to have such good fortune.

One day, Ant younger brother pushed a cart of rice past Miss Cicada's tree and suddenly heard a melodious singing voice. Ant thought, "This must be when Miss Cicada is singing and making merry again. I should advise her to work." So Ant climbed up the tree.

Miss Cicada felt very bad after hearing Ant's advice and said to Ant, "I know, but it's already late today. I'll start working tomorrow." Ant happily said goodbye to Miss Cicada and went back to pushing rice.

The next day, Ant carried a bag of flour and passed by Miss Cicada's tree again. Miss Cicada was still singing. Ant climbed up to advise her again. Miss Cicada saw Ant coming and quickly said, "I know, I know! It's already late today, I'll start working tomorrow!" Ant climbed down the tree very disappointed. Carrying the flour, he left.

On the third day, Ant carried a load of sugar and passed by Miss Cicada's tree again. He still heard the melodious singing voice. Ant knew that Miss Cicada was a lazy creature who loved leisure and hated work, so he stopped being friends with her and carried the sugar away.

On the fourth day, the fifth day, the sixth day... When Ant passed by Miss Cicada's tree, he heard Miss Cicada still singing loudly: "I know! I know!"

The Strength Contest Between the Sun and the Wind 196

— Weaker

丨Original from (Japanese Elementary School Reader)丨

Once upon a time, the sun and the wind wanted to have a strength contest. They decided that whoever could make the traveler take off his coat would be the winner. The wind started first.

The wind said, "How about it? Let me roll up and show you!" So the wind blew fiercely. At that time, the traveler became colder and colder as the wind blew, so he wore his coat tighter and tighter.

This time it was the sun's turn. The sun showed its gentle face from the gaps in the clouds and shone its warm sunlight. The traveler felt warm on his ears and finally took off his coat, so the wind was considered to have lost.

Unclean Things 197

— Ren Wei

Summer has arrived, and the thermometer has risen to about one hundred degrees. Cold drink stalls are set up on every street. Many people, because they are thirsty, buy things that flies have landed on to eat, regardless of whether the food is clean or not. Who knows that eating these things is very dangerous. Acute epidemic diseases such as cholera and vomiting are caused by these unclean things!

The above is all known to everyone. Other things, such as ladybugs, horsehair wasps, wall lizards, and jumping spiders, also feed on small insects. The small insects they eat are harmful to us humans, so carnivorous insects are mostly beneficial insects. Children, how should we protect these insects that are beneficial to humans?

Home Animal Garden 198

— Han Sheng

Summer vacation has started, and the weather is really hot. Younger brother is a smart child. He set up a home animal garden.

What is this home animal garden like?

On the lawn in front of the house, there are flowers and trees, and also a wooden frame with potted plants. The site of the animal garden is here.

Younger brother hung the parrot and its cage on the holly tree, moved the goldfish bowl to the middle of the lawn, and moved Linlin's kennel from the door, letting it bark beside the kennel. He filled a large lead basin with water and caught the ducklings to swim in it. He also drove the white rooster, fat hen, and chicks from behind the house. He also borrowed a parrot and four canaries from the neighbor, hanging them on the loquat tree with their stands and cages. Our white-spotted big cat was also caught by younger brother and tied with a rope, because he was afraid it would bite the ducklings and chicks. It was out of luck.

Our home animal garden opened, and younger brother and younger sister invited many children to visit us here.

Next to each animal, we tied a piece of cardboard with its name written on it with a rope for the visitors' reference.

We gave each visiting child four crackers. We didn't give them out the second time. We also prepared an autograph book, and everyone who came had to sign their name on it. This home animal garden was closed after two days because the weather was too hot and we wanted to go to the shade of the trees in the park to play.

Names of Several Types of Flying Vehicles 199

— Dong Xun

Nowadays, the sky has become a means of transportation for humans! In countries with advanced science, many flying vehicles fly continuously day and night in the air between two or more cities. Even in our China, we can often see several Chinese and foreign joint venture airplanes flying in the air.

In China, there are many terms that are not unified. Taking just the terms for flying vehicles as an example: when we see a monoplane land aircraft flying in the air, everyone shouts: "Look! A flying boat is coming!" But when a biplane seaplane is moving in the sky, everyone shouts: "Look! A flying boat is coming!" They call both things "flying boats." This is really a mistake! Children, can you tell the difference clearly?

In fact, it is very easy to distinguish the types of flying vehicles. Now, I have drawn several types that I know. In this way, after looking at it, you will generally not confuse the names of flying vehicles again.

The flying vehicles in this picture, except for airships, flying boats, and balloons, are the rest we have seen in the air. In addition, there are gliders... Because there are no perfect and good results, they are not included. As for the names of the uses of airplanes, such as warplanes, bombers, commercial airplanes, etc., are also not included.

Carnivorous Insects 200

— Gong Ji Tang

Most insects live by eating the leaves and branches of plants; another part of insects live by eating meat. However, the meat they eat is not like the beef and pork that we humans eat, but rather small animals, especially insects. Here are a few common examples:

1. Dragonflies: They have transparent and powerful wings, fly in the air, and use their sharp and strong mouthparts to catch small insects as food. Their larvae are called water nymphs and also catch small insects such as mosquito larvae for food.

2. Mantises: They use their first pair of legs, which have turned into knives, to catch insects for food.

3. Spiders: They also catch insects for food. Their tool for catching insects is a web made of silk.

The Danger of Playing with "Simple Balloons" and Its Remedies 201

— Yan Xin Quan

In the previous issue of the Children's Weekly, there was an article by Mr. Zi Jing on how to make and play with "simple balloons"; according to Mr. Zi Jing's purpose, it was nothing more than to make children understand the function of air, which is very admirable. However, this way of playing has not been said completely, because the balloon will inevitably be blown away by the wind after it rises into the air, even if it is blown a mile away. I remember six or seven years ago, several people (adults) were also playing with this thing. After the balloon rose into the air and was blown away by the wind, each person dispersed when they could no longer see the balloon. The next day, a message came from a village saying that a sky fire had burned down more than a dozen thatched houses.

Therefore, children who play this balloon in the open space must tie a thin string under the balloon to prevent danger, and at most let it rise to a height of one or two zhang. This way of playing is already very interesting and also much safer.

Sweat 205

— Bing Yu

After we have worked or because of the hot weather, our skin will be covered in damp sweat. But what is sweat made of? I will briefly explain the common knowledge about sweat as follows:

(1) Sweat Secretion: Sweat comes from the sweat glands in the dermis and subcutaneous tissue. There are blood vessels around the sweat glands. Blood from the blood vessels is filtered out to the sweat gland opening on the surface of the skin and excreted from the body. There are about 2.5 million sweat glands in our whole body, so there are densely distributed sweat glands in every part. However, the amount of sweat varies depending on the season and the person. Ordinary adults produce about half a liter (1 liter equals 1.08 Chinese sheng) to less than 1 liter per day. (2) Sweat Composition: Sweat is mostly water and contains fat, salt, urea, etc. Therefore, sweat tastes salty. After sweating, the urea and fat decompose and turn into ammonia, causing sweat odor. (3) Sweat Function: Sweating removes useless components from the blood, cleans the blood, and regulates body temperature. In summer, the body of an average person can reduce body temperature by 400 to 500 calories (a unit of heat) after sweating, making them feel cool. Therefore, the surface of the body is cool in summer. Chinese doctors use Chinese medicine to dispel heat for patients with fever. After the patient takes the medicine, they break out in a lot of sweat, which can reduce the fever. This is also the reason. (4) The Relationship Between Sweat and Nerves: In general, obese people have a thick layer of fat under their skin to maintain body temperature. In summer, because they release more body heat, they sweat more. If we are suddenly unhappy in spirit, our blood vessels contract, our nerves become excited, and our skin turns pale. Due to the effect of the sweat-producing nerves, we sweat cold sweat. Death sweat near the time of death is for this reason. Also, if the body is unwell, it will definitely constantly stimulate the sweat-producing nerves and cause more sweating. When this kind of sweat is produced, the body will feel uncomfortable. Also, if a person suffers from blood sweat disease, their sweat will contain more blood. If a person suffers from diabetes, their sweat will contain more sugar. These are all improper sweating. (5) The Relationship Between Sweat and Shoes and Socks: There are many sweat glands on the soles of the feet. The sweat secreted is confined by the tightness of the shoes and socks and is not ventilated. Therefore, when the shoes and socks are taken off, the fat and urea in the sweat decompose faster and the odor spreads everywhere. Therefore, feet should be washed and socks changed every day. (6) The Occurrence of Sweat Stains: If there is a lot of sweat on the surface of the skin and it stays on the skin for a long time without being washed away, the skin will be stimulated by the sweat and red sweat stains will appear. If not prevented, they will spread quickly. Therefore, after sweating, we should wash and disinfect our bodies and use powder to absorb moisture. That way, we can keep our bodies clean and prevent diseases.

Women's Corner

The New Meaning of Motherhood 206

— Xu Xi Zhen

——To New Women——

Progressive Ladies:

You must know this: an accurate proposition is not afraid of multifaceted observation; one plus one equals two: no matter how you calculate it, it will not be wrong. Are we not trying to explain the path to true women's liberation from all aspects? Whether women want to achieve equality of social status, economic independence, liberation from etiquette, reasonable standards of sexual morality, etc., the path is still very clear, there is only one: to build a new society.

Originally, the social system is the greatest mystery of mankind, it is the spring in the clock, once it is solved and fixed, everything will become a problem. However, the process of improving a social system is very difficult; the biggest problem is the lack of a new standard. All the old society's standards of morality, good and evil, virtue and vice are necessarily unsuitable for the new society; and although establishing another new standard is urgently needed, it is also very difficult.

We should make the discussion more concrete: for example, we now hear the terms "virtuous mother and good wife" under the old three obediences and four virtues, and we will definitely regard it as like poison, right? However, that old society, even if it has no ill intentions, should ask us, "Don't new people need virtuous mothers and good wives, but need inferior wives and evil mothers?"

In this way, not only will the people who ask questions in the old society become more and more confused, but I am afraid that even we ourselves will find it difficult to answer specifically?

But in fact, this is a non-problem problem, answer briskly: "In the new era, in the new society, we also need virtuous mothers and good wives, just as we needed them in the old society. The only difference is that the meaning of the two words virtuous and good has a fundamental difference": that is to say: "The new and old views and standards of virtuous and good are absolutely different."

If we want to escape from the feudal social system, we should also understand the nature of the feudal society and the foundation of its standards of good and evil. The old society's economic distribution method was uneven, and benefits and power always fell on the side that enjoyed the economic surplus, so women were always the possessions of men. Their only requirements for women were obedience and educating a group of women who were their descendants. Therefore, the "goodness" of a wife lies in the three obediences and four virtues, and the "virtue" of a mother lies in her ability to educate her children well. A virtuous and good mother should not only be subject to and obey others herself, but also have to educate sons who dominate other women and daughters who obey other men.

This means that they are calling on every woman to build the strong walls that imprison herself and the fetters that bind herself.

What a cruel tragedy.

Mothers are worthy of pride, because they hold the fate of the next generation; and also worthy of fear, because they also hold the fate of the next generation.

The so-called virtuous mothers and good wives that we have seen before today are all big fools who teach the next generation of men to dominate the next generation of women, and teach the next generation of women to obey the next generation of men.

We hope (and believe) that the foolish thing of building walls to imprison oneself will never be seen again in the world in the future. In the new society of the future, we also need virtuous mothers and good wives, we want smart new mothers who "tear down" the walls themselves!

However, as I said earlier, modern women's liberation is not a comedy of "male struggle," but a big social problem (simply a common problem for both men and women). New women, in addition to their own struggles, should shift the eyes of their descendants to the unreasonableness of the social system.

"Make your children a group of people who are useful to the public!"

Only this kind of maternal education is reasonable, progressive, and expected by the new society.

The new good wife will know how to liberate herself from the shackles of the family and go to society; the new virtuous mother will know how to teach her descendants to continue her difficult journey.

That way, you see: don't we also need virtuous mothers and good wives? However, this is reasonable.

Progressive ladies, be proud, be fearful, because you are holding the fate of the next generation.

On Nurseries and Public Childcare: A Third Discourse 207

— Zi Jiu

And a Response to Mr. Shi Shi

Regarding "Nurseries and Public Childcare," Mr. Shi Shi has commented twice, and I have also written twice to discuss it. In the July 13th issue of this newspaper's local supplement, there was another article by Mr. Shi Shi, "A Third Discussion on Nurseries and Public Childcare." After reading the entire article, I feel that Mr. Shi Shi has failed to adopt an objective attitude and examine the reasons held by those who argue against his views. Instead, he repeatedly expresses his own subjective opinions. This has diminished the nature of the discussion, and I was initially unwilling to write further on the matter. However, I believe that childcare is a facet of women's issues and a significant aspect of social issues. Readers will want to evaluate the rights and wrongs of the debate on this issue. Indeed, in the July 31st issue of the "Shishi Xinbao" in the "Modern Women" section, there was an article by Ms. Tan Shuangping titled "The Problem of Nurseries and Public Childcare," which provided a detailed refutation of Mr. Shi Shi's "Third Discussion on Nurseries and Public Childcare." Besides being pleased to find a kindred spirit, I would like to add some further points, jointly questioning Mr. Shi Shi and seeking public opinion from those concerned about social issues.

(1) After reading Mr. Shi Shi's three articles, the fundamental error lies in equating modern "public childcare" with the ancient Spartan state's ownership of children. He is thus fearful that once children are publicly cared for, they will lose their parents, and parents will be forever deprived of the joy of having their children around. However, common sense tells us that "public childcare" is not like that at all. Simply put, it means that the state spends money to provide scientific and organized childcare for the people, in the same way that the state spends money to run primary schools, middle schools, and universities. In that case, how does a child's enrollment in a publicly funded nursery sever their connection with their parents? This is precisely to benefit families and respect the meaning of life, and is certainly not against the natural order of procreation. Furthermore, take the Soviet Union, which has already implemented public childcare, for example. Have parents there completely abandoned their children, or do children lose their parents as soon as they enter a nursery? Mr. Shi Shi seems to believe that the Soviet Union's current foster care methods are not truly public childcare – of course, their methods may still be in the process of improvement, but this is a matter of method and irrelevant to the issue itself. However, in his first article on "Nurseries and Public Childcare," Mr. Shi Shi once said, "Public childcare in Europe and America is quite active and is being effectively implemented with success..." Now, Mr. Shi Shi suddenly denies this, stating, "Currently, I am afraid that only the Soviet Union has nurseries organized under the principle of public childcare, and their foster care is only 'boarding' and does not conform to the true meaning of public childcare." It is truly unknown what Mr. Shi Shi's so-called public childcare actually is.

(2) Having nurseries does not necessarily mean that it is public childcare, but countries that implement public childcare must universally establish nurseries. This is inevitable. The state should create labor nurseries in response to social needs, which can be considered the precursor to implementing public childcare. For the sake of liberating women and for the future of society, public childcare is truly necessary. Moreover, reality tells us that there are already nurseries established in China, which clearly demonstrates the need for them. Even incomplete institutions such as foundling homes, orphanages, and homes for poor children are so much in demand by society. Would complete nurseries under public childcare not be even more popular? Therefore, I believe that unless men are selfish and believe that all women only have the instinct to raise children, and force the future masters of the country to receive poor education, then with a clear understanding of the progress of society, they should recognize the necessity of implementing nurseries and public childcare. Therefore, the question is not whether public childcare should be implemented under the current Chinese system, but whether public childcare can be fully implemented. In the present situation where all education is still commercialized, it is of course impossible to universally implement public childcare. However, we cannot oppose it simply because it is impossible.

(3) In his most recent article, Mr. Shi Shi admits that the existing nurseries in Europe and America are only improved foundling homes. In that case, the infant mortality rate in Parisian public childcare cited by Mr. Shi Shi from the writings of the famous American sociologist Edward Alsworth Ross cannot be considered an example of true public childcare.

In summary, I am not trying to make things difficult for Mr. Shi Shi. It is just that Mr. Shi Shi's great arguments contain considerable errors. As Ms. Tan Shuangping said, "For the sake of upholding the truth," it is necessary to engage in analytical discussion with Mr. Shi Shi. This is my original intention in writing three articles to refute his arguments. I hope the readers can make a fair judgment and also express their opinions on this issue.

A Great Woman Among Oppressed Nationalities 208

— Le Ji

——Mrs. Naidu——

When speaking of great figures among oppressed nationalities, I believe everyone will remember Mahatma Gandhi of India. The person I want to introduce now is a woman who is contemporary to him, from the same country, and possesses the same spirit as him. Who is this person? It is Mrs. Naidu.

Although Mrs. Naidu is a woman in India, an oppressed country that also devalues women, her spirit and deeds will exist alongside the history of India, and she is truly comparable to Gandhi. Like Gandhi, she rejected the idea of class consciousness early on. She was born into the high-ranking Brahmin caste, but in her own marriage, she set an example by breaking free from the constraints of class.

She is a great writer and a great politician at the same time. In 1924, she became a member of the Royal Society of Literature in England, and she is the only woman in all of India who has served as the president of the Indian National Congress. She also attended the Indian Round Table Conference held in London in 1932 with Gandhi. Imprisonment cannot break her determined spirit. She once said: As long as my life exists, and as long as my blood flows in this hand, I will never give up the struggle for freedom. Arise, my warriors! Although I am just a woman, a poet, in terms of women, I give you weapons of faith and boldness, and an indomitable spirit; in terms of poets, I call out singing banners, the sound of bugles on the battlefield, how will I awaken you men, so that everyone can break free from the shackles of slavery!?

Her appearance is short and vigorous, and her eyes are especially bright. Her spirit seems to ignite emotions, but she treats people with great peace. She completely expresses her inner suffering in poetry. She has a smart mind, a mind that flashes like lightning. She often engages in the pursuit of beauty, and she often transforms everything in the world into golden words and golden deeds. Her life has almost been consumed by curiosity about various things. She can be deeply worried and wildly happy. Her laughter is even more mysterious, a unique talent she possesses. Her laughter may be a kind of mask. However, it is this laughter that enables her mind to see things clearly when her heart cannot bear it. Therefore, she can laugh loudly when reciting her wild songs, and she can laugh when she is enthusiastic. She once wrote in a letter, "Among the talents that Heaven has given me, the one I value most is laughter." In fact, in her environment, only laughter can overcome everything and tolerate everything.

She is already fifty-five years old this year and the mother of four grown children. Although her body is aging day by day, her spirit of fighting for national freedom never slackens. She truly deserves to be a great woman among oppressed nationalities!

Divorce and Educational Bankruptcy 210

— Dan Lun

| Regarding the Divorce of Ms. C in H City |

Ms. C is a highly respected teacher in H City. Not long ago, she married a male friend she had known for many years. However, after a few months of marriage, she discovered that there was no true love between them; and the man also had marital disputes elsewhere. Emotionally and rationally, there was no need to continue living together, so she directly and frankly proposed a divorce to the man. Although the man was very concerned about his image, he also knew that it was impossible to force her, and their divorce was handled unconditionally.

This was originally a very ordinary, very normal, and very bright thing, and should not have caused any criticism. However, this society is a male-centered society. Women being divorced or abandoned in tangible and intangible ways is common, while divorce initiated by women seems to be a reversal of heaven and earth, and should not happen at all. Because this society is a society that follows old customs and is content with the status quo, even if the couple has different dreams in the same bed, or are incompatible like ice and charcoal, or have become mortal enemies, they should still maintain the form of the family on the surface, taking care of face and reputation (although the author does not know what this face is, or what this reputation is), until they grow old together. At the same time, this society is also a society that despises women, believing that women are born with the centuries-old inheritance of "marrying a chicken, following a chicken, marrying a dog, following a dog" – which is what most people consider to be the virtue of women. They definitely do not have the ability to be independent and self-reliant, and they are definitely not allowed to have self-awareness.

Therefore, when a self-aware divorce event like that of Ms. C occurs, it will naturally cause a lot of criticism. Because she is engaged in education, some people are even heartbroken and denounce it as "educational bankruptcy." Educational bankruptcy and divorce are clearly as different as a horse's head and an ox's mouth, but they insist on linking them together. The author is not smart enough to find the relationship between the two!

Of course, educational bankruptcy is a social problem; at the same time, divorce is also a social problem, but these are just two individual social problems, and there is no causal relationship to speak of. If you say that because Ms. C is engaged in education, and people engaged in education get divorced, it is educational bankruptcy, then this is truly a ridiculous logic!

Regarding marriage, we do not advocate rapid separations and reunions like changing Qin for Chu in the morning and evening, but we also never support puppet partners who are seemingly united but actually estranged. In feudal Chinese families, there are more or less living widows, and more or less women who are trampled on, abandoned, and deceived. I hope they will raise their heads like Ms. C and settle accounts with the other party! Whether they are working, staying at home, engaged in education, etc....

If a woman engaged in education who initiates a divorce due to self-awareness is considered "educational bankruptcy," then we might as well hope that women who stay at home, work, or do other things will have a family bankruptcy, industrial bankruptcy, or | | bankruptcy.

Common Sense for Summer Families—Infant Diarrhea 211

— Du Bu

Intestinal inflammation is most likely to occur in infants around one year old.

The most common diarrheal disease in young children is intestinal inflammation, which is most common among infants around one year old. As for artificially fed infants, intestinal inflammation can easily occur even at four or five months of age, especially as a result of irregular feeding schedules and random feeding of various foods, resulting in chronic nutritional disorders. Special attention must be paid to the diarrheal condition of such poorly developed infants.

Symptoms of intestinal inflammation

When intestinal inflammation occurs in infants, the initial symptom is only an increase in the number of bowel movements. It does not cause acute symptoms like dysentery and bacillary dysentery. The progress is relatively slow, so it is often overlooked. If appropriate treatment is applied urgently at the beginning of the illness, it can be quickly cured. If no attention is paid and it is treated lightly, fever will begin after a few days, accompanied by vomiting, increased diarrhea, dry mouth, and deep breathing, eventually leading to poisoning and an incurable disease. At this time, the body weight drops sharply, consciousness is blurred, convulsions occur frequently, and life is in danger. The possibility of death accounts for more than two-thirds.

The digestive function of infants is already weaker than usual in the summer heat. If diarrhea occurs, the digestive power of infants with nutritional disorders will be reduced from one-third to one-half at the beginning of the illness. If they are still given the usual amount of food at this time, the condition will inevitably worsen, eventually leading to fever and poisoning symptoms.

It is better to pay attention to food and drink than to give medicine.

Therefore, when an infant suffers from diarrhea, it is necessary to stop giving food and drink, or at least reduce it by two-thirds from the usual amount, and quickly seek medical treatment in order to preserve its lovely little life. The doctor will examine the strength of the infant's gastrointestinal tract and determine the appropriate food and amount, and pay attention to the symptoms at any time to ensure safety. At that time, food is sometimes more effective than medicine. However, it is definitely not something that can be handled casually by someone without medical training.

The effect of prevention cannot be absolutely guaranteed.

For diseases such as dysentery and bacillary dysentery, preventive injections are usually used, or the internal medicine "Valve Qing" is taken. However, whether injections or internal medicines are administered, daily health care should still be paid attention to, and everyday life should be treated with caution to raise infants with hygienic habits, because no other preventive method has a 100% effect.

Correspondence

Dear Editor:

I am a traitor to my family, and I have been away for six years. But now I am very shaken and hesitant day and night, and I specially ask for your help.

I entered hell (forgive me! I never want to mention that hateful word) in the eighth year of the Republic of China, in the so-called "semi-new and semi-old" way at that time. That is, the parents have already decided, and then the mother will take a photo for me to see. The air that night was very mysterious and solemn, the windows were tightly closed, and the mother's throat was trembling, with no trace of a smile. I remember clearly that I didn't see anything, I didn't nod, but I didn't shake my head either. God! Why did I lose even the sense of shaking my head at that time? Just because I didn't shake my head, my living life was cut off with a single blow at the young age of sixteen.

After that, I really don't want to mention life afterwards. My every word and deed are flawed. They talked about the lewd behavior of someone else's daughter, and the collapse of someone else's career every day, and laughed gleefully at every misfortune, and I couldn't not laugh, and it wasn't possible to occasionally shed a tear when I laughed. I couldn't read newspapers or novels, I couldn't go back to my mother's house or visit my classmates and sisters, and I couldn't even correspond with them, because female students are mostly not good things (their common saying). I couldn't recite a poem of hatred, and I couldn't sing a few songs to relieve my worries. I am completely a living dead person. I gave birth to two children, and I am not allowed to participate in any opinion on education. The children are either beaten for no reason, or taken to the theater, gambling place, or brothel. I am heartbroken all day long for my two children ten times more than I am for myself.

The Revolutionary Army pacified Jiangnan, and my courage was somehow strengthened by the sound of liberation. One night, while the room was filled with the smell of alcohol, I took my two children and left home. Unexpectedly, before I could find a way to make a living, I was chased back fiercely. This time, I suffered not only mental punishment.

I endured physical and mental pain for my children for a long time. When I could no longer bear it, I quietly left. I looked back at the dark clouds of my hometown day by day, as if being chased by a demon, so I walked farther and farther day by day. Now, I am three thousand miles away from home. Now I am teaching a group of rural children who originally had no opportunity to study, but because I only ask the village for two coarse meals a day, I have maintained it for three years. I treat the children as my own, giving them all my enthusiasm. The children also treat me as their second mother, giving me extra respect and intimacy.

I want to rely on courage to make another place my home, and to treat children who have dropped out of school as my children, and to continue to do so for the rest of my life. But recently I have been shaken, shaken badly. Because now everyone is advocating the trend of virtuous mothers and good wives, I don’t know whether doing this and going home to be a virtuous mother and good wife is more upright? I am not a virtuous mother and good wife, is there still the value of a "person"? In this world, I want to choose the thing with the greatest meaning to do. If a virtuous mother and good wife is the only highest morality for women, then I can only painfully abandon this group of lovely and pitiful poor children, and return to that useless family of mine. However, that would be so painful! That's why I am hesitant, hesitant, day and night. I can't find clear discussions in the countryside, and I hope you can guide me!

Li Jinying, July 30th

Ms. Jinying:

We are very sympathetic to your past behavior, and we admire your enthusiasm twenty-four minutes. You are a warrior against the old etiquette and evil forces. You have been a virtuous mother, and a virtuous mother of many children. This meaning is much more upright than being a living dead at home. Why do you have to go home again? Everyone knows that there are two sexes on Earth, and women are qualified to be wives and mothers, but new women | | especially you who have already left, of course don't need to go home again, no, go back to the home you think is useless. The greatest meaning of life still lies in being independent: economically independent and personality independent! Under this conclusion, you don't have to hesitate. Brave you, don't be blinded by that charming smoke screen again, and be taken to be a prisoner again. I wonder what you think? Reporter
